tathā jyotiṣṭome dīkṣārthābhyaṅge śrūyate- aghṛtaṃ devānāṃ, mastu pitṝṇām, niṣpakvaṃ manuṣyāṇām, tadvā etatsarvadevatyaṃ yannavanītam, yannavanītanābhyaṅkte sarvā eva devatāḥ prīṇāti' iti ।
mastu dadhibhavaṃ maṇḍam ।
niṣpakvaṃ śirasiprakṣeptumīṣadvilīnaṃ navanītaṃ takraṃ vā ।
darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ puroḍāśaśrapaṇe śrūyate-"yo vidagdhaḥ sa naiṛtaḥ, yo aśṛtaḥ sa raudraḥ, yaḥ śataḥ sa daivaḥ, tasmādavidahatā śrapayitavyaḥ sa daivatvāya'' iti ।
vidagdho atyantapakvaḥ ।
aśṛto apakvaḥ ।
tatra - varhiṣi samūlacchedasya, abhyaṅge navanītasya puroḍāśe yathocitapākasya ca vidheyatayā sarvamavaśiṣṭaṃ stāvakam ।
nivītavicārasyaivāyaṃ prapañcaḥ ।
evam ayatpūrṇe tanmanuṣyāṇām' ityatrāpi draṣṭavyam ।
tacca cāturmāsyeṣu mahāpitṛyajñe apitṛbhyo agniṣvāttebhyo abhivānyā gordugdhe mantham'ityatra vatsarahitāyā abhidānīśabdābhidheyāyā dhenvā dugdhe piṣṭaṃ prakṣipya kriyamāṇe manthane śrūyate- ayatpūrṇe tanmanuṣyāṇāmupari, ardho devānām, ardhaḥ pitṛṇāma, ardha upamanthati, artho hi pitṝṇām' iti ।
tatra pātrasyādhobhāgarūpeṇār dhena parimite dugdhe manthanasya kartavyatvātsor'dho vidhīyate ।
sa ca pūrṇādivākyena stūyate ।
akarma kratusaṃyuktaṃ saṃyogān nityānuvādaḥ syāt ।
vidhir vā saṃyogāntarāt ।

-
aṣṭamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
anṛtaṃ na vadedvaidhaḥ puṃdharmo vānuvaidagīḥ ।
sakratau puṃsi śuddhevā kratau yadvā vidhiḥ kratau ।
anṛtoktaiḥ pumarthatvāttanniṣedhastathābidhaḥ ।
smārtānubādaḥ puṃskratvoḥaśrutiprakriyayovaṃśāt ।
nā'khyāte puruṣānuktiḥ kratāveva prayājavat ।
satyoktiniyamādanyaḥ saṃyogo ataḥ kratau vidhiḥ ।

darśapūrṇamāsaprakaraṇe śrūyate- anānṛtaṃ vadet' iti ।
tatra-puruṣadharmatvenāyaṃ pratiṣedho vidhīyate ।
kutaḥ ।
pratiyogino anṛtavadanasya puruṣadharmatayā tanniṣedhasyāpi puruṣadharmatvenaiva vidhātavyatvāt ।
avadet' ityākhyātaṃ tāvatkartṛvācakam ।
tenā'khyātena kartṛḥ pratīyamānatvāt ।
puruṣasyā'khyātapratyayavācyatve sati prakṛtyarthasya vadanasya puruṣadharmatvaṃ yuktam ।
aprakṛtipratyayau pratyayārthe saha brūtaḥ, tayostu pratyayaḥ prādhānyena' iti śābdikairuddhoṣaṇāt ।
vadanasya puruṣadharmatve tanniṣedhasyāpi puruṣadharmatvaṃ yuktam ।
anyathā bhinnaviṣayatve bādhakatvaṃ na syāt ।
tasmātpurūṣavācakākhyātaśrutyā prakaraṇaṃ bādhitvā puruṣārtho ayaṃ pratiṣedho vidhīyate ।
astyeva smārtaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ- iti cet ।
tarhi tasyaitacchrutivākyaṃ mūlamastu ।
tasmāt- puruṣārthaḥ- ityekaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
ākhyātaśruteḥ prakaraṇasya cāvirodhāya kratuyuktapuruṣadharmo astu ।
nahyetadvākyaṃ smṛtermūlam ।
bhinnaviṣayatvāt ।
smṛtiścopanayanamārabhyā'maraṇaṃ puruṣasyānṛtaṃ pratiṣedhati ।
tanmadhyapatitatvātkratāvapi smārto niṣedhaḥ prāpta eva ।
tata ubhayārtho apyayaṃ pratiṣedho na vidhīyate, kiṃtvanūdyate- iti dvitīyaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
ākhyātena bhāvanābhidhīyate ।
kartā tu tadavinābhūtor'thātpratīyate ।
ataḥ śrutyabhāvātkevalena prakaraṇena prayājādivadārādupakārakaḥ kratāveva niviśate ।
na ca tatrāpi vidhīyate, kiṃtu sārvatrikasya niṣedhasya kratāvapi prāptatvādanūdyate- iti tṛtīyaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
asatyameva vadet, natvanṛtam' iti yo ayaṃ smārtāniyamarūpaḥ puruṣārthaḥ saṃyogaḥ, tasmādayamanyaḥ kratvarthaḥ saṃyogaḥ ।
ato aprāptatvādvidhīyate ।
etadvyatikrame kratoreva vaiguṇyam, na tu puruṣasya pratyavāyaḥ ।
ato atra kratugāmi prāyaścittam ।
puruṣārthaniyamātikrame tu puruṣasyaiva pratyavāyo na kratorvaiguṇyam ।
tatra smārte prāyaścitam- iti viśeṣaḥ ।
ahīnavat puruṣas tadarthatvāt ।
prakaraṇaviśeṣād vā tadyuktasya saṃskāro dravyavat ।
vyapadeśād apakṛṣyeta ।

navamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
jañjabhyamānamantroktiḥ puṃso dharmaḥ kratoruta ।
vākyādādyaḥ prakriyayā dvitīyo astvaviruddhayā ।

darśapūrṇamāsaprakaraṇe śrūyate-'prāṇo vai dakṣaḥ ।
apānaḥ kratuḥ ।
tasmājjañjanyamāno brūyāt- mayi dakṣakratū-iti, prāṇāpānāvevā'smanyadhatta' iti ।
gātravināmena vidāritamukhaḥ puruṣo jañjabhyamānaḥ ।
tasya vākyānmantroktiḥ pratīyate ।
vākyaṃ ca prakaraṇādbalīyaḥ ।
tasmāt- kevalaṃ puṃdharmaḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
kratāvapi jañjabhyamānapuruṣasaṃbhavena vākyaprakaraṇayorvirodhābhāve satyubhābhyāṃ kratuyuktapuruṣasaṃskāratvāvagamāt ।
śaṃyau ca sarvaparidānāt ।

-
daśamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
viprāyāvagurenneti kratvartho vā pumarthatā ।
phalavatkratusāṃnidhyātkratvarthaḥ pūrvamantravat ।
yātanāparihārasya niṣedhaphalatocitā ।
niṣedho ayaṃ pumarthatvātprakriyāto apakṛṣyatām ।

darśapūrṇamāsaprakaraṇe śrūyate- ayo brāhmaṇāyāvagurettaṃ śatena yātayet ।
tasmādbrāhmaṇāya nāvagureta' iti ।
tatra- yathā pūrvādhikaraṇe mantrapāṭhasya phalarahitasya phalavati kratāvaṅgatvaṃ prakaraṇenāvagamyate, evamatrāpi brāhmaṇāvajñāniṣedhasya kratvaṅgatvam- iti cet ।
na ।
vaiṣamyāt ।
pūrvatra hi - ātmani māṇāpānadhāraṇaṃ mantroccāraṇaphalaṃ na saṃbhavati ।
tasya prāgeva siddhatvāt ।
iha tu- avagoraṇe śatasaṃvatsarayātanāmupanyasyāvagoraṇaniṣedhā- dyātanāparihārasya niṣedhaphalatvamucitam ।
tasmāt- niṣedhasya kevalapuruṣārthatayā prakaraṇā dutkarṣo yuktaḥ ।
prāgaparodhān malavad vāsasaḥ ।
annapratiṣedhāc ca ।

ekādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
na saṃvadeta malavadvāsasetyapi pūrvavat ।
pumarthaḥ syātkratau kvāpi saṃvādasyāprasaktitaḥ ।

darśapūrṇamāsaprakaraṇe śrūyate- amalavadvāsattā na saṃvedata' iti ।
-asya niṣedhasya prakaraṇā tkratvaṅgatvam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
aprasaktapratiṣedhaprasaṅgāt ।
yasya vratye ahani patnvanālambhukā bhavati, tāmaparudhya yajeta' iti rajasvalāyā niḥsāraṇena kratau tatsaṃvādasyāprasaktiḥ ।
tasmāt- kevalapuruṣārthasyāsya prakaraṇādutkarṣaḥ ।
aprakaraṇe tu taddharmas tato viśeṣāt ।
adravyatvāt tu śeṣaḥ syāt ।
vedasaṃyogāt ।
dravyasaṃyogāc ca ।
syād vāsya saṃyogavat phalena saṃbandhas tasmāt karmaitiśāyanaḥ ।

-
dvādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
hiraṇyaṃ varṇavadbhārye kratvaṅgaṃ bharaṇaṃ bhavet ।
hiraṇyasaṃskṛtirvātra varṇo vota pumarthatā ।
vaidikatvātkratusmṛtyā tadaṅgaṃ karmakārake ।
prādhānyātsaṃskṛtivarṇo guṇo astu vidhilāghavāt ।
anārabhya śrutatvena niyatā na kratusmṛtiḥ ।
ataḥ pumarthatā svargaḥ kalpyo anyadvāstu rātrivat ।

anārabhya śrūyate- atasmātsuvarṇe hiraṇyaṃ bhāryam ।
suvarṇa eva bhavati ।
duvarṇo asya bhrātṛvyo bhavati' iti ।
tatra-yadetacchobhanavarṇopetahiraṇyadhāraṇaṃ tasya vaidikakriyārūpatvena kratusmārakatvātkratvaṅgaṃ dhāraṇam- ityekaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
kratvaṅgatve api nā'rādupakārakam, kiṃtu kratṛgataṃ hiraṇyaṃ dhāraṇena saṃskriyate ।
abhāryam' ityatra ṇyatpratyayasya karmaṇi vihitatvena karmakārakasya hiraṇyasya prādhānyāvagamāt - iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
varṇaviśiṣṭadhāraṇavidhāne gauravāddhāraṇasahitaṃ hiraṇyamanūdya śobhanavarṇamātraṃ vidheyam- iti tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
tredhāpi- kratvartho vidhiḥ, na tu puruṣārthaḥ- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- yaddhikratuprakaraṇe śrutam, tasyāsti niyamena kratusmārakatvam ।
idaṃ tvanārabhyādhītam ।
na cātra hiraṇyaṃ juhvādivatkratāvavyabhicaritam, yena kratusmṛtirniyamyeta ।
nanu saṃskāryatvānyathānupapattyā kratupraveśaḥ syāt ।
nahi dhāraṇena saṃskṛtasya hiraṇyasya laukikaḥ kaścidupayogo asti- iti cet ।
na ।
kratāvapyupayogābhāvāt ।
- kratūpayogo api kalpyate- iti cet ।
na ।
akratūpayogitvena saṃskāryatvam, tena ca kratūpayogaḥ' ityanyonyāśrayatvāt ।
ataḥ kratau niyantumaśakyatvātpuruṣārthamidaṃ dhāraṇam ।
na cātra phalābhāvaḥ ।
viśvajinnyāyena svargasya kalpyatvāt ।
athavā rātrisanne yathā vākyaśeṣeṇārthavādena śrutā pratiṣṭhā kalatvena kalpitā tathātrāpi asuvarṇa eva bhavati, durrvaṇo asya bhrātṛvyaḥ' ityarthavādagataṃ phalamastu ।
tasmāt- puruṣārtho dhāraṇavidhiḥ ।
śeṣāḥ prakaraṇe aviśeṣāt sarvakarmaṇām ।
homās tu vyavatiṣṭher annāhavanīyasaṃyogāt ।
śeṣaś ca samākhyānāt ।

-
trayodaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
yenertsetkarmaṇā tatra jayāhome akhilārthatā ।
vaidikeṣveva vā sarvaśeṣo asaṃkocakatvataḥ ।
homa āhavanīye syātkṛṣyādiṣu na so asti hi ।
tenānārabhyapāṭhe api vaidikeṣveva te jayāḥ ।

anārabhya śrūyate- ayena karmaṇertset ।
tatra jayāṃ juhuyāt ।
rāṣṭrabhṛto juhoti ।
abhyātānāñjuhoti' iti ।
īrtsedṛddhimicchet ।
acittaṃ ca svāhā' ityādayo jayāḥ aṛtāṣāḍ' ityādayo rāṣṭrabhṛtaḥ ।
aagnirbhūtānām'- ityādayo abhyātānāḥ ।
tatra- vaidikakarmaṇeva laukikakṛṣyādikarmaṇāpyṛddheriṣyamāṇatvāt, saṃkoce kāraṇāmāvājjayādihomaḥ sarvaśeṣaḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
ayadāhavanīye juhvati tena so asyābhīṣṭaḥ prītaḥ' iti vākyena homamuddiśyā' havanīyavidhānāt ।
kṛṣyādau tadabhāvādvaidikeṣveva jayādihomaḥ ।
doṣāt tv iṣṭir laukike syāc chāstrād dhi vaidika na doṣaḥ syāt ।
arthavādo vānupapātat tasmād yajñe pratīyeta ।

-
caturdaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
aśvapratigraheṣṭistu dāturityabhidhāsyate ।
dānadvaye laukike vā vaidike vā bhavediyam ।
aviśeṣāddvayoryadvā na deyaḥ kesarītyataḥ ।
niṣedhāllaukikāttatra prāyaścittiriyaṃ bhavet ।
na jalodarahetutvaṃ pramitaṃ laukike kvacit ।
vaidike tu śrutaṃ tasmāttatprāyaścittaye atra sā ।

idamāmnāyate-'yāvato aśvānpratigṛhṇīyāttāvato vāruṇāścatuṣkapālānnirvapet' iti ।
tatra apratigrahaśabdo dānaparaḥ' ityanantarameva vakṣyate ।
tatra-viśeṣāśravaṇāllaukikavaidikadānayorubhayo rapyasāviṣṭiḥ- ityekaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
ana ketariṇo dadāti' iti smṛtyā mitradāyādādibhyaḥ prītyā kriyamāṇaṃ lokikamaśvadānaṃ niṣiddham ।
tadanuṣṭhāne prāyaścittarūpeyāmiṣṭiḥ- iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
avaruṇo vā etaṃ gṛhṇāti yo aśvaṃ pratigṛhṇāti' ityaśvadāne jalodakhyādhirūpo dṛṣṭadoṣo varuṇagrahavākyenocyate ।
na ca laukikasyāśvadānasya taddhetutvaṃ pramitam ।
vaidikasya tu janmāntaraviṣayaṃ doṣaśravaṇam ।
ato vaidikadāne seṣṭiḥ prāyaścittam ।
asti hi vaidikamaśvadānam ।
avaḍavā dakṣiṇā' ityādiśravaṇāt ।
acoditaṃ ca karmabhedāt ।
sā liṅgād ārtvije syāt ।

-
pañcadaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
yāvataḥ pratigṛhṇīyādaśvāṃstāvatya iṣṭayaḥ ।
pratigrahīturdāturvā syādādyo astu yathāvidhi ।
asaṃjātavirodhyarthavādāddātuḥ prajāpateḥ ।
iṣṭiḥ śrutā tato dāturṇijarthe api vidhiṃ nayet ।

pūrvodāhṛte vākye apratigṛhṇīyāt' iti vidhipadaśravaṇātpratigrahīturiṣṭiḥ- iti cet ।
na ।
upakramarūpeṇārthavādena dātustadiṣṭipratīteḥ ।
upakramaścaivaṃ śrūyate- aprajāpativaruṇāyāśvamanayat, sa svāṃ devatāmārchat ।
sa paryadīryata, sa etaṃ vāruṇaṃ catuṣkapālamapaśyat, taṃ niravapat, tato vai sa varuṇapāśādamucyata' iti ।
anayadvattavān ।
sa ca dātā prajāpatiḥ svakīyāṃ varuṇadevatāṃ jalodararogapradāṃ prāptavāna ।
tena ca rogeṇa grastaḥ sa prajāpatirvidīrṇo bhūtvā rogaparihārāyeṣṭiṃ kṛtvā rogādamucyata, ityatra- dāturiṣṭiḥ- ityavagamyate ।
asaṃjātavirodhyupakramānusāreṇa vidhāvakapadamapi apratigrāhayet' ityevamantarbhāvitaṇijarthaparatayā vyākhyaiyam ।
pānavyāpac ca tadvat ।
doṣāt tu vaidike syād arthād dhi laukike na doṣaḥ syāt ।

-
ṣoḍaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
somavāmicarurloke vede vendriyasaṃkṣayaḥ ।
dṛṣṭadoṣo lokike ato vamane vihitaścaruḥ ।
adoṣo vamanāyaiva loke pānaṃ śrutau punaḥ ।
jaraṇāya tato vāntidoṣaśāntyai bhaveccaruḥ ।

idamāmnāyate- asaumendraṃ caruṃ nirvapecchyāmākaṃ somavāminaḥ'' iti ।
tatra-laukike somavamane vihito ayaṃ caruḥ ।
kutaḥ ।
avi vā eṣa indriyeṇa vīryeṇa vyṛdhyave yaḥ somaṃ vamati' iti dṛṣṭadoṣamupanyasya tacchāntaye caruvidhānāt - iti cet ।
maivam ।
loke dhātusāmyārthino vamanāyaiva somasya pāne sati vamanasya doṣahetusvābhāvāt ।
vede tu ahinva me gātrā harivaḥ' ityanena mantreṇa jarayituṃ somaḥ pīyate ।
tatra vamanaprāyaścittārtho ayaṃ caruḥ ।
tatsarvatrāviśeṣāt ।
svāmino vā tadarthatvāt ।
liṅgadarśanāc ca ।

saptaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
ṛtvijāṃ vamane apyeṣa karturevota varjanāt ।
viśeṣasyāgrimo maivaṃ kartureva niruptitaḥ ।

aīdṛśasya somasya vamane caruḥ' iti viśeṣasyābhāvādṛtvijāṃ yajamānasya ca vamane sarvatrāsau caruḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
ayo vamati sa nirvapati' iti nirvapturvamanaṃ carunimittam ।
nirvaptā ca yajamānaḥ ।
ṛtviyo nirvaptṛtve adhikāryantaratvaprasaṅgāt ।
tasmāt- yajamānasyaiva vamane caruvidhiḥ ।
(aṣṭādaśe - āgneyāṣṭākapālacarordvyavadānamā-
trasya hotavyatādhikaraṇe sūtrāṇi -)
sarvapradānaṃ haviṣas tadarthatvāt ।
niravadānāt tu śeṣaḥ syāt ।
upāyo vā tadarthatvāt ।
kṛtatvāt tu karmaṇaḥ sakṛt syād dravyasya guṇabhūtatvāt ।
śeṣadarśanāc ca ।

aṣṭādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
yāge havistyajetkṛtsnaṃ ko apyaṃśaḥ śiṣyate api vā ।
devārthatvādyajetsarve śiṣyate dviravattataḥ ।

aāgneyo aṣṭākapālaḥ' ityatra kṛtsno api puroḍāśo agnaye tyaktavyaḥ ।
taddhitena kṛtsnasyāgnidevatāsaṃbandhāvagateḥ ।
tyāgamantareṇaitadanupapattiḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
advirhaviṣo avadyati' ityavadānadvayaṃ śrūyate ।
avadeyaṃ cāṅguṣṭhaparvamāvam ।
tathā ca kalpasūtrakāraḥ- aāgneyasya puroḍāśasya madhyādaṅguṣṭhaparvamātramavadānaṃ tiraścīnamavadyati' iti ।
tato haviṣaḥ sakāśādaṅguṣṭhaparvadvayamātraṃ khaṇḍayitvā tyaktavyam ।
itaraccheṣaṇīyam ।
devatāsaṃbandhaścāṃśadvāreṇāpyupayujyate ।
aprayojakatvād ekasmāt kriyerañ śeṣasya guṇabhūtatvāt ।
saṃskṛtatvāc ca ।
sarvebhyo vā kāraṇāviśeṣāt saṃskārasya tadarthatvāt ।
liṅgadarśanāc ca ।

ekonaviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
śeṣātsviṣṭakṛdekasmātsarvebhyo vaikataḥ kṛte ।
śāstrārthasiddhiḥsarvebhyaḥ kāryaḥ saṃskārasāmyataḥ ।

darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate- aśeṣātsviṣṭakṛte samavadyati' iti ।
tatra-āgneyādīnāṃ trayāṇāṃ haviṣāṃ madhye yasya kasyacidekasya haviṣaḥ śeṣādavadātavyam ।
tāvataiva śāstrārthānuṣṭhānasiddhaḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
upayuktaṃ haviḥ saṃskartumidamavadīyate ।
saṃskāraśca sarveṣvapi haviḥṣu samānaḥ ।
tasmāt- sarvebhyo haviḥśeṣebhyaḥ sviṣṭakṛdanuṣṭheyaḥ ।
ekasmāc ced yathākāmyam aviśeṣāt ।
mukhyād vā pūrvakālatvāt ।

viṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
yadaikasmāttadā mukhyaniyātirnota vidyate ।
nāśruterasti mukhyātikramaṇe hetvabhāvataḥ ।

aekasmādeva haviḥśeṣātsviṣṭakṛt' iti yaḥ pūrvādhikaraṇe pūrvapakṣaḥ, tasminpakṣe niyāmakasyāśrutatvāt-
yasmātkasmācciddhaviḥśeṣāt- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- prathamātikrame mānābhāvātprathamahaviḥśeṣeṇaiva saṃskārāsiddhāvitaratra prāptyabhāvādasti niyatiḥ ।
bhakṣāśravaṇād dānaśabdaḥ parikraye ।
tatsaṃstavāc ca ।
bhakṣārtho vā dravye samatvāt ।
vyādeśād dānasaṃstutiḥ ।

-
ekaviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
idaṃ brahmaṇa ityaktiḥ krayārthā bhakṣaṇāya vā ।
bhakṣāśruteḥ krayārthāto yatheṣṭaṃ tairniyujyatām ।
devatāya samastasya kḷptatvātsvāmitā na hi ।
śeṣasya pratipattyarthe bhakṣaṇaṃ tatra yujyate ।

caturdhākṛtapuroḍāśasya bhāgānyajamāna evaṃ nirdiśet- aidaṃ brahmaṇaḥ, idaṃ hotuḥ, idamadhvaryoḥ, idamagnīdhaḥ, iti ।
so ayaṃ nirdeśa na bhakṣaṇārthaḥ ।
bhakṣaṇasyāśrutatvāt ।
tato bhṛtidānena tānṛtvijaḥ parikretumayaṃ nirdeśaḥ kṛtaḥ ।
krayaśca tadaṅgīkārānusāreṇa svalpenāpyupapadyate ।
tasmātsvakīyā bhāgāstairicchayopayoktuṃ śakyāḥ- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- aagneya juṣṭaṃ nirvapāmi' iti kṛtsnasya haviṣo devatārthe saṃkalpitatvena tatra yajamānasya svāmitvābhāvānna yuktaḥ parikrayaḥ ।
bhakṣaṇaṃ tu pratipattyarthatvādyuktam ।
avaśiṣṭasya yaḥ ko apyupayogaḥ pratipattiḥ ।
puroḍāśasya bhakṣaṇāhatvādbhakṣaṇena karmakarāṇāmṛtsāhajananācca bhakṣaṇārtho ayaṃ nirdeśo yujyate ।
iti śrīmādhavīye jaiminīyanyāyamālāvistare tṛtīyādhyāyasya caturthaḥ pādaḥ

atha tṛtīyādhyāyasya pañcamaḥ pādaḥ ।
ājyāc ca sarvasaṃyogāt ।
kāraṇāc ca ।
ekasmin samavattaśabdāt ।
ājye ca darśanāt sviṣṭakṛdarthavadasya ।
aśeṣatvāt tu naivaṃ syāt sarvādānād aśeṣatā ।
sādhāraṇyān na dhruvāyāṃ syāt ।
aktatvāc ca juhvāṃ tasya ca homasaṃyogāt ।
camasavad iti cet ।
na codanāvirodhād dhaviḥ prakalpanāc ca ।
utpannādhikārāt sati sarvavacanam ।
jātiviśeṣāt param ।
antyam arekārthe ।

-
pañcamapādasya prathamādhikaraṇamāracayati
upāṃśuyājadravyeṇa śeṣakārye bhavenna vā ।
bhaveddhavirbhyaḥ sarvebhya ityuktyā prāpitatvataḥ ।
uktājyadravyaśeṣastu bhāvyupastaraṇādikṛt ।
ato na pratipattyarhaḥ śeṣakārye tataḥ katham ।

dhrauvādājyājupāṃśuyājārthamavadāne kṛte taccheṣeṇa dhrauveṇa dravyeṇa sviṣṭakṛdādikaṃ śeṣakārya kartavyam ।
kutaḥ ।
atadyatsarvebhyo havirbhyaḥ samavadyati' iti vākyena prāpitatvāt- iti cet ।
maivam ।
kṛtārthadravyaśeṣo hyupayogāpekṣaḥ pratipattimarhati ।
dhrauvaṃ tvājyaṃ na kṛtārtham ।
tena kartavyānāmupastaraṇādīnāṃ sadbhāvāt ।
tasmāt - na tena śeṣakārye bhavati ।
sākaṃprasthāyye sviṣṭakṛd iḍaṃ ca tadvat ।

-
dvitīyādhikaraṇamāracayati-
ākrāmansaha kumbhībhirasti śeṣakriyā na vā ।
juhvāvadānātprakṛtāviva śeṣakriyocitā ।
kumbhīṣu śeṣāsaṃsiddhaḥsākaṃprasthāyyakarmaṇi ।
na sviṣṭakṛdiḍaṃ kāryamagnīdhaḥ strukpradānataḥ ।

asākaṃprasthāyīyena yajeta paśukāmaḥ' iti vihite karmaṇi śrūyate- asaha kumbhībhirabhikrāmannāha' iti ।
tatra catasṛbhirdadhipayaḥkumbhībhiḥ sahā'havanīyadeśe abhikramaṇa mātraṃ śrutam ।
na tu tatra kumbhībhirhomaḥ śrutaḥ ।
tathā satyasya karmaṇaḥ sāṃnāyyavikṛttitvājjuhvā kumbhībhyo avadāya hotavyam ।
hutaśeṣeṇa ca sviṣṭakṛdādikaṃ sāṃnāyyaśeṣeṇaiva kartavyam- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- nātra kumbhīṣu hutaśeṣaḥ sidhyati ।
sāṃnāyyavajjuhvā tadavadānābhāvāt ।
aagnīdhe strucau pradāya saha kumbhībhirabhikrāman' ityuktyā juhūpabhṛtoḥ prattatvādabhikramaṇasya homārthatvācca kumbhībhireva dadhipayasorhome sati kumbhīmātrāmavaśiṣyate, na tu haviḥśeṣaḥ ।
tatra kutaḥ śeṣakāryam ।
sautrāmaṇyāṃ ca graheṣu ।
tadvac ca śeṣavacanam ।

tṛtīyādhikaraṇamāracayati-
sautrāmaṇyāṃ grahe sviṣṭakṛdādyasti na vāsti tat ।
śeṣaṇānna surākṣīrayoranyatropayogataḥ ।

sautrāmaṇināmake yāge śrūyate - apayograhāḥ surāgrahāśca gṛhyante' iti ।
tatra prakṛtigata somadyaheṣviva śeṣakārye sviṣṭakṛdādikamasti ।
na cātra pūrvavaccheṣābhāvaḥ ।
aucchinaṣṭi, na sarve juhoti' ityavaśeṣayitavyatvaśravaṇāt- iti cet ।
maivam ।
avaśiṣṭasyānyatropayogaśravaṇāt ।
abrāhmaṇaṃ parikrīṇīyāduccheṣaṇasya pātāram' iti śrūyate ।
ayadi brāhmaṇaṃ na vindeta, valmīkavapāyāmavanayet' iti ca ।
aśatātṛṇāyāmavaneyat' iti ca ।
śatacchidrā kumbhī śatātṛṇā ।
tasmāt- nāsti sviṣṭakṛdādikam ।
dravyaikatve karmabhedāt pratikarma kriyeran ।
avibhāgāc ca śeṣasya sarvān pratyaviśiṣṭatvāt ।

-
caturthādhikaraṇamāracayati-
rathaṃtarādibhirminnā indrāsteṣāṃ na bhidyate ।
puroḍāśastatra śeṣakārye kiṃ bhidyate na vā ।
bhidyate karmaṇāṃ bhedāccauddakaiḥ pṛthaguktitaḥ ।
śeṣasya sarvatulyatvāttatkārye sakṛdiṣyatām ।

aya indriyakāmo vīryakāmaḥ syāt, tametayā sarvapṛṣṭhayā yājayet' iti vihitāyāmiṣṭau ṣaḍindrā evaṃ śrūyante- aindrāya rāthaṃtarāya, indrāya bārhatāya, indrāya vairājāya, indrāyaśākvarāya, indrāya raivatāya' iti ।
tatra svarūpeṇaiko apīndraḥ pṛṣṭhastotreṣu ṣaṭsu vihitānāṃ ṣaṇṇāṃ rathaṃtarādi sāmnāṃ saṃbandhena viśeṣyamāṇaḥ ṣoṭhā bhidyate ।
tāsāṃ sarvāsāmindradevatānāmeka eva puroḍāśo vidhīyate- advādaśakapālaḥ puroḍāśo bhavati ।
vaiśvadevatvāya' iti ।
tasmiṃśca puroḍāśe proktadevatābhyaḥ pṛthakpṛthakpradānāya bahubhyaḥ pradeśebhyo avadānaṃ śrūyate- asamantaṃ paryavadyati' iti ।
tatra devatābhedena pradānabhedena ca karmaṇāṃ bhede sati pṛthagatideśātsviṣṭakṛdiḍādi śeṣakārye ṣaṭkṛtvaḥ pṛthakkartavyam - iti cet ।
maivam ।
śeṣasyaikatvena tatpratipatteḥ pṛthaktvāsaṃbhavāt ।
tasmāt- sakṛdeva kāryam ।
aindravāyave tu vacanāt pratikarma bhakṣaḥ syāt ।

pañcamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
aindravāyavaśeṣasya sakṛdbhakṣa utāsakṛt ।
pūrvanyāyātsakṛtprāptau dvirbhakṣo vacanādbhavet ।

jyotiṣṭome yo ayamaindravāyavagrahaḥ' tatra saṃskāryasya somasyaikatvātsakṛdeva śeṣakāryam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
adviraindravāyavasya bhakṣayati, dvirhyetasya vaṣaṭkaroti' iti vacanādvirbhakṣaṇam ।
some avacanād bhakṣo na vidyate ।
syād vānyārthadarśanāt ।
vacanāni tv apūrvatvāt tasmād yathopadeśaṃ syuḥ ।

ṣaṣṭhādhikaraṇamāracayati -
someṣvabhakṣo bhakṣo vā na bhakṣo grahahomataḥ ।
alpokterasti śeṣo asya bhakṣo apūrvavacobalāt ।

somayāgeṣu śeṣabhakṣo nāsti, ayadgrahāñjuhoti' iti kṛtsnagraheṇā'huti śravaṇātkumbhīṣviva śeṣābhāvāt- iti cet ।
maivam ।
aalpaṃ juhoti' iti viśeṣavacanāccheṣaḥ sidhyati ।
tadbhakṣaṇaṃ tvapūrvārtha pratipādakavacanebhyo avagamyate ।
aāśvinaṃ bhakṣayanti' dviraindravāyavasya bhakṣayanti' asadasi bhakṣayanti' ityādīni vacanānyapūrvārtha pratipādayanti ।
tato bhakṣavidhānādasti someṣu bhakṣaḥ ।
camaseṣu samākhyānāt saṃyogasya tannimittattvāt ।

saptamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
kiṃ praitu hotuśrcamasa ityabhakṣo atha bhakṣaṇam ।
abhakṣo anuktito hotuśrvamasetyākhyayāstu tat ।

jyotiṣṭome śrūyate- apraitu hotuśrvamasaḥ, pra brahmaṇaḥ, prodvātṝṇāṃ, pra yajamānasya, prayantu sadasyānām' iti ।
tatra- vacanāmāvādabhakṣaḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
samākhyāgate camasaśabde bhakṣaṇasya pratīyamānatvāt ।
acamvate bhakṣyate somo asminpātraviśeṣe' iti hi tadvyutpattiḥ ।
tasmāt-ḥasti tadbhakṣaṇam ।
udgātṛcamasamekaḥ śrutisaṃyogāt ।
sarve vā sarvasaṃyogāt ।
stotrakāriṇāṃ vā tatsaṃyogād bahuśruteḥ ।
sarve tu vedasaṃyogāt kāraṇād ekadeśe syāt ।

-
aṣṭamādhikaraṇamāracayati -
prodvātṝṇāmiti hyeka udgātā bhakṣayeduta ।
sarve api kiṃvā subrahmaṇyenoktāḥ sāmagāyinaḥ ।
sahitāstena te vā'dya udgātṛśrutito akhilāḥ ।
bahutvādgānayogena tṛtīyo rūḍhibādhite ।
yoge samākhyayā daṇḍinyāyādantyo atra bhāṣyagaḥ ।
sadasi sthityabhāvena tṛtīyo vātiṃkoditaḥ ।

pūrvodāhṛtavākye aprodvātṝṇām' ityatraikasyaiva bhakṣaḥ ।
udvīthaśabdābhidheyāyāḥ sāmabhakteru- dgātaryudgātṛprātipadikasya rūḍhatvāt - ityekaḥ pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
audgātṝṇām' ityasya bahutvasyaikasmi nnasaṃbhavādudgātropalakṣitāḥ ṣoḍaśartvijaḥ sarve api bhakṣayeyuḥ- iti dvitīyaḥ ।
udgīthaprastāvaprati hārāntāmabhāgānudvātṛprastotṛpratihartāraḥ prayogakāle gāyanti ।
audutkarṣeṇa gāyanti' iti yogenodvātārastrayo bhakṣayeyuḥ- iti tṛtīyaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
arūḍhiryogamapaharati' iti nyāyādeka evodgātā ।
tena ca bahuvacanopapattaye pratyāsannā upalakṣyante ।
pratyāsattiśca prastotṛpratihartroriva subrahmaṇyasyāpyasti ।
sāmavedādhyāyitvena subrahmaṇyāhvānarūpe tadīyakarmaṇyapyaudgātrasamākhyāyāḥ sattvāt ।
tasmāt- asubrahmaṇyena sahitāścatvāraḥ sāmagā bhakṣayeyuḥ'- ityayamantyaḥ pakṣo bhāṣyakārasyābhimataḥ ।
vārtikakārastu - sadaso bhakṣaṇasthānatvātsubrahmaṇyasya sadasyapraveśāttena virahitā avaśiṣṭāḥ sāmagā bhakṣayanti- iti tṛtīyaṃ pakṣamaṅgīcakāra ।
grāvastuto bhakṣo na vidyate anāmnānāt ।
hāriyojane vā sarvasaṃyogāt ।
camasināṃ vā saṃnidhānāt ।
sarveṣāṃ tu vidhitvāt tadarthā camasiśrutiḥ ।

-
navamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
kiṃ syāccamasināmeva hāriyojanabhakṣaṇam ।
sarveṣāṃ vāgrimasteṣāṃ pūrvavākyeṇa saṃnidheḥ ।
lipsante sarva eveti hāriyojanavākyataḥ ।
prāvastuto apyasti bhakṣaścamasitvamakāraṇam ।

aharirasi hāriyojanaḥ' ityanena mantreṇa gṛhyamāṇo graho hāriyojanaḥ ।
hotṛbrahmādaya ścamasimaḥ ।
yastu caturṇo hotṝṇāṃ madhye caturtho grāvastunnāmake asti, nāsau camasī ।
tatra camasināmeva hāriyojanabhakṣaṇam ।
kutaḥ-"yathācamasamanyāṃścamasāṃścamasino bhakṣayanti, athaitasya hāriyojanasya sarva eva lipsante' ityatra pūrvavākye camasināṃ saṃnihitvenottaravākye sarvaśabdena teṣāmevābhidhātavyatvāt ।
ato nāsti grāvastutastatra bhakṣaḥ- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- athaśabdenaivakāreṇa ca camasimātraśaṅkāmapodya vākyena vihitasya sarvamakṣaṇasya saṃnidhimātreṇa saṃkocāyogādasti grāvastuto api bhakṣaḥ ।
tasmāt- camasitvaṃ na bhakṣaṇe kāraṇam ।
vaṣaṭkārāc ca bhakṣayet ।

-
daśamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
ādyamakṣo vaṣaṭkarturvidhiḥ prāthamya eva kim ।
kiṃvā tadyuktabhakṣe syādvaṣaṭkāranimittake ।
aprāpteragrimo maivaṃ samāsasthityasaṃbhavāt ।
viśiṣṭasya vidhistasmādvaṣaṭkāro api kāraṇam ।

avaṣaṭkartuḥ prathamabhakṣaḥ' ityevaṃ śrūyate ।
vaṣaṭkartā hotā ।
tasya bhakṣaṇaṃ samākhyāyā prāptam ।
prāthamyaṃ tvaprāptamiti tadevātra vidhiyate - iti cet ।
maivam ।
aprathamabhakṣaḥ' ityasya samastapadatvena ayo bhakṣaḥ, sa prathamaḥ' ityeyaṃ vicchidyānve tumayogyatvātprāthampaviśiṣṭabhakṣaṇamatra vidhīyate ।
tasminbhakṣaṇe vaṣaṭkāraḥ kāraṇam ।
homābhiṣavābhyāṃ ca ।

-
ekādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
ākhyāvacovaṣaṭkārā eva kiṃ bhakṣahetavaḥ ।
kiṃvābhiṣavahomau ca tatrā'dyo astūktayā diśā ।
havirdhāne abhiṣutyātha hutvā sadasi bhakṣayet ।
iti śrutatvatastau ca bhakṣahetū yathettare ।

apraitu hotuścamasaḥ' ityatra samākhyā bhakṣahetuḥ ।
hāriyojane vākyam ।
avaṣaṭkartuḥ prathamabhakṣaḥ' ityatra vaṣaṭkāraḥ ।
ityevamuktatvātraya eva bhakṣahetavaḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
ahavirdhāne grāvabhirabhiṣutyā'havanīye hutvā pratyañcaḥ paretya sadasi bhakṣānbhakṣayanti' iti śrūyate ।
uttaravedyāḥ pratīcīne sadasaḥ prācīne maṇḍale amiṣavaḥ ।
uttaravedyāṃ homaḥ ।
sadasi bhakṣaṇam ।
tatra- abhiṣavahomayorvacanāntaraprāptayoravidheyatayā tau nimittatvenānūdya bhakṣaṇaṃ vidhīyate ।
tasmāt- samākhyādivadetayorapi bhakṣaṇahetutvamasti ।
pratyakṣopadeśāc camasānām avyaktaḥ śeṣe ।
syād vā kāraṇabhāvād anirdeśaś camasānāṃ kartus tadvacanatvāt ।
camase cānyadarśanāt ।

-
dvādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
hetusaṃghe vikalpaḥ kiṃ bādho vātha samuccayaḥ ।
sāmyādvikalpo bādhyantāṃ sāvakāśāḥ samākhyayā ।
naiva vācanikaṃ bādhyaṃ bhakṣaṇe atra vibhāgaśaḥ ।
siddhevikalpo no yuktaḥ svīkāryo ataḥ samuccayaḥ ।

apraitu hotuścamasaḥ, pra brahmaṇaḥ'- ityatra cimasiṣu samākhyā bhakṣaṇe hetuḥ ।
avaṣaṭkartuḥ prathamabhakṣaḥ' ityatra vaṣaṭkāro hoturbhakṣahetuḥ ।
ahavirdhāne grāvamirabhaṣutyā'havanīye hutvā sadasi bhakṣayanti' ityatrābhiṣavasahito homo adhvaryorbhakṣahetuḥ ।
tatra camasavaṣaṭkārayoḥ saṃgho hotari prāptaḥ ।
camasābhiṣavasaṃgho adhvaryau prāptaḥ ।
tatra hetudvayasya samānabalatvādvikalpe satyanyatara nimittakṛtamevaṃ bhakṣaṇam- ityādyaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
vaṣaṭkārādihetoścamasetaragrahe sāvakāśatvānniravakāśayā camasisamākhyayā tadbādhe sati camasiṣu pākṣikamapi vaṣaṭkārādi hetukaṃ bhakṣaṇaṃ nāsti- iti dvitīyaḥ pakṣaḥ ।
avaṣaṭkartuḥ' ityādivākyasya prabalatvātsamākhyayā bādho na yuktaḥ ।
miravakāśatayā sāpi prabalā- iti cet ।
tarhi pramāṇadvayena pṛthagbhakṣaṇe vihite samuccayo abhyupeyaḥ, na ca vrīhiyavavadvikalpaḥ ।
tatra puroḍāśāniṣpādanasya dṛṣṭaprayojanasyaikatvāt ।
iha tu niyamādṛṣṭārthe bhakṣaṇam ।
taccādṛṣṭaṃ yathāvacanaṃ dvividham ।
tasmātsamuccayaḥ ।
ekapātre kramād adhvaryuḥ pūrvo bhakṣayet ।
hotā vā mantravarṇāt ।
vacanāc ca ।
kāraṇānupūrvyāc ca ।

-
trayodaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
ekapātre kimadhvaryuradyātpūrvaprutetaraḥ ।
taddhaste pātrasaṃsthānāttasya prathamabhakṣaṇam ।
pāhi hoteva naḥ pūrvamiti mantreṇa pūrvatā ।
vaṣaṭkartustadukteśca nyāyabādhyaṃ vaco nahi ।

ekasminpātre vahanāṃ kvacidvihitaṃ bhakṣaṇam- tatra- adhvaryuḥ prathamaṃ bhakṣayetpātrasaṃnidhānāt - iti cet ।
maivam ।
liṅgavākyābhyāṃ hotuḥ prathamamakṣāvagamāt ।
ahoteva naḥ prathamaḥ pāhi' iti ṛtvijo adhvaryu saṃbodhyaivaṃ prārthayante- ayathā hotāsmattaḥ pūrve bhakṣayitvā śeṣapradānenāsmānpālitavān, tathā tvamapi vāhi' iti ।
tadetaddhotuḥ prathamabhakṣe liṅgam ।
vākyaṃ caivamāmnātam- avaṣaṭkartuḥ prathamabhakṣaḥ' iti ।
tatra viśiṣṭavidhānātprāthamyamipa sidhyati ।
na caitadvacanaṃ pātrasaṃnidhirūpeṇa nyāyamātreṇa bādhituṃ śakyam ।
tasmāt - hotā prathamaṃ bhakṣayet ।
vacanād anujñātabhakṣaṇam ।

caturdaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
nānujñāpūrvako bhakṣastatpūrvo vātra lāghavāt ।
ādyo nānupahūtena peya ityuktito antimaḥ ।

anujñābhakṣayordvayoranuṣṭhitau gauravādbhakṣamātram - iti cet ।
maivam ।
atasmātsomāṃ nānupahūtena peyaḥ' iti vacanenānujñāyā āvaśyakatvāt ।
tadupahūta upahvayasvety anenānujñāpayel liṅgāt ।

pañcadaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
kimanujñā laukikoktyā vedoktyā vā yathā tathā ।
aviśeṣādupahvānamantraliṅgāttu vaidikī ।

aupahūta upahvayasya'- ityayaṃ mantro liṅgena mantramanujñāyāṃ viniyuṅkte ।
tasmāt- vaidikoktyā tadanujñānam ।
tatrārthāt prativacanam ।

-
ṣoṣṭhaśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
upahvayasvopahūta ityaśeṣo dvayorbhavet ।
anujñānujñāpanayorathavāsau vibhajyate ।
vibhāgakaraṇābhāvādaśeṣaśrcenna liṅgataḥ ।
upahvayetvanujñaptāvanujñāne tathetaraḥ ।

aupahūta upahūvayasva' ityasminmantre madhyamapuruṣekavacanānto bhāgaḥ paścātpaṭhito api praścasamatvātprathamabhāvinyanujñāpane samarthaḥ ।
prathamaikavacanāntastu prathamapaṭhito apyuttarasamānatvā tpaścādbhāvinyāmanujñāyāṃ samarthaḥ ।
tasmāt- liṅgena vibhajya viniyujyate ।
tadekapātrāṇāṃ samavāyāt ।

saptadaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
upahvānamaśeṣāṇāmuta syādekapātriṇām ।
adṛṣṭahetorādyaḥ syāddṛṣṭādhikyādito antimaḥ ।

anujñāpanasyādṛṣṭaṃ prayojanam ।
tacca vibhinnapātreṣvapi samānam- iti cet ।
na ।
dṛṣṭaprayojanasya sadbhāvāt ।
sādhāraṇe vastuni kathaṃcidbhāgādhikye aparādho bhavati ।
ato nyūnādhikatvaparihāranimittamanujñāpanamekapātriṇāmeva ।
yājyāpanayenāpanīto bhakṣaḥ pravaravat ।
yaṣṭur vā kāraṇāgamāt ।
pravṛttatvāt pravarasyānapāyaḥ ।

-
aṣṭādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
hoturyājyāpanītau kiṃ na vaṣaṭkārabhakṣayoḥ ।
apanītirutāpāyo nāpanītirvibhedataḥ ।
yajamānena yaṣṭavyaṃ na vineṣṭirvaṣaṭkṛtim ।
vaṣaṭkāro yājyayātaḥ sahāpaityadanaṃ tathā ।

jyotiṣṭoma ṛtuyājanāmakeṣu yāgeṣvāmnāyate-"yajamānasya yājyā so abhipreṣyati- hotaretadyaja- iti, svayaṃ vāṃ niṣadya yajati"iti ।
hautre kāṇḍe samāmnātā yājyāḥ samākhyayā hotuḥ prāptāḥ ।
tāsu kācidyājyā hoturapanīya yajamānasya vidhīyate ।
tato yajamānaḥ svecchayā hotāraṃ vā preṣyati, svayaṃ vā yājyāṃ paṭhati ।
tatra tvapāṭhapakṣe yājyā hoturapanīyate, na tu vaṣaṭkārabhakṣāvapanīyete ।
tayoryājyāyāmanantarbhāvāt ।
ato hotā vaṣaṭkaroti bhakṣayati ca iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- asvayaṃ vā niṣadya yajati' iti pakṣasvīkārādyajamānena svayaṃ yāgaḥ kartavyaḥ ।
sa ca yāgo vaṣaṭkāramantareṇa na saṃbhavati ।
ayājyāyā adhi vaṣaṭkaroti' iti tadvidhānāt ।
nanu- yajamāno yājyāṃ paṭhatu, hotā vaṣaṭkarotu- iti cet ।
maivam ।
aanavānaṃ yajati' iti yājyāvaṣaṭkārayormadhye śvāsaniṣedhenaikakartṛkatvāvagamāt ।
ato yājyayā saha vaṣaṭkāro hoturapaiti ।
tadapāye vaṣaṭkāranimitto bhakṣaśca hoturapetya yajamāne niviśate ।
phalacamaso naimittiko bhakṣavikāraḥ śrutisaṃyogāt ।
ijyāvikāro vā saṃskārasya tadarthatvāt ।
homāt ।
camasaiś ca tulyakālatvāt ।
liṅgadarśanāc ca ।

-
ekonaviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
nyaprodhapiṣṭaṃ somasya sthāne kṣatriyavaiśyayoḥ ।
bhakṣamātre vikuryāttatsomayāge api vā tathā ।
bibhakṣayiṣayā vākyamupakramyopasaṃhṛtam ।
bhakṣaṃ yacchediti tato vikāro bhakṣamātragaḥ ।
phalākhyacamasenāsau yajeteti śrutatvataḥ ।
ijyāyāṃ ca vikāro asti yāgārthā bhakṣasaṃskṛtiḥ ।

jyotiṣṭome śrūyate- ayadi rājanyaṃ vaiśyaṃ vā yājayet, sa yadi somaṃ bibhakṣayipet, nyagrodhastibhinīrāhṛtya tāḥ saṃpiṣya dadhanyunmṛjya tamasyai bhakṣaṃ prayacchet, na somam' iti ।
stibhinyo mukulāni ।
tatra- upakramopasaṃhārayorbhakṣaviṣayatvādbhakṣamātre somaḥ piṣṭena vikriyate - iti cet ।
maivam ।
ayadānyāścamasāñjuhvati, athaitasya darbhataruṇakenoṣahatya juhoti' iti śrutam ।
tatra phalacamasarūpeṇa yathoktapiṣṭena yāgamaṅgīkṛtya taruṇakaguṇo vidhīyate ।
kiṃca - iṣṭadravya saṃskāro hi bhakṣaḥ ।
sa ca yāgamantareṇānupapannaḥ ।
tasmāt- yāge api vikāraḥ ।
anuprasarpiṣu sāmānyāt ।
brahmaṇā vā tulyaśabdatvāt ।

-
viṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
rājasūye kvacitkartuścamaso daśabhirjanaiḥ ।
makṣyaḥ kiṃ tatra rājanyā bhakṣakā brāhmaṇā uta ।
ādyo bhānātsaṃkhyayaikajaiterviprāḥ śataṃ daśa ।
camasānadyurityuktyā rājapātraṃ ca vipragam ।

rājasūye daśapeyanāmake yāge śrūyate- adaśa daśaikaikaṃ camasamanuprasarpanti' iti ।
tatra yajamānasya rājanyasya yaścamasaḥ, so ayaṃ rājanyaireva daśabhirbhakṣaṇīyaḥ ।
kutaḥ ।
adaśa' iti saṃkhyāyā jātyekatvapratibhānāt ।
tathā hi - daśapoyasya jyotiṣṭomavikṛtvātprākṛtaṃ dharmajātaṃ codakena prāptam ।
prakṛtau ca - yajamānacamasasya bhinnajātibhirbhakṣaṇaṃ nāsti, ityatrāpi tathaiva praptam ।
yadi- atra adaśa' iti viśeṣo vidhīyate, tarhi prākṛtaṃ bhakṣasaṃkhyāmātraṃ nivartatām, natvekajātitvam ।
tasmāt- rājanyo yajamāno anyai rājanyairnavabhiḥ saha bhakṣayet- iti prāpte,- brūmaḥ- prakṛtitaḥ prāpteṣu daśasu camaseṣu bhakṣaṇāyāmuprasarpatāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ adaśa, daśa, iti vīpsayā praticamasaṃ daśasaṃkhyāṃ vidhāyārthasiddhāṃ śatasaṃkhyāmanūdya saṃkhyeyānāṃ sarveṣāṃ brāhmaṇyaṃ vidhīyate -'ṅgha śataṃ brāhmaṇāḥ pibanti' iti ।
tathā sati- yajamānasyāpi rājanyasya yatra camasabhakṣo nāsti, tatra kuto anye rājanyā bhakṣayeyuḥ ।
tasmāt - brāhmaṇā eva bhakṣakāḥ ।
iti śrīmādhavīye jaiminīyanyāyamālāvistare tṛtīyādhyāyasya pañcamaḥ pādaḥ

atha tṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭhaḥ pādaḥ ।
sarvārtham aprakaraṇāt ।
prakṛtau vādviruktatvāt ।
tadvarjaṃ tu vacanaprāpte ।
darśanād iti cet ।
na codanaikārthyāt ।
utpattir iti cet ।
na tulyatvāt ।
codanārthakārtsnyāt tu mukhyavipratiṣedhāt prakṛtyarthaḥ ।

-
ṣaṣṭhapādasya prathamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
prakṛtau vikṛtau vā syādyasya parṇetyasau vidhiḥ ।
prakṛtāveva vā tulyādvacanādubhayorasau ।
juhūmāśritya parṇatvavidhiḥ prakṛtimātragaḥ ।
codakenobhayaprāptervikṛtau vidhinātra kim ।

anārabhya śrūyate- ayasya parṇamayī jūhūrbhavati, na sa pāpaṃ ślokaṃ śṛṇoti' iti ।
tatra- avyabhicaritakratusaṃbandhavatīṃ juhūmāśritya taddhetuḥ parṇavṛkṣo vākyena vidhīyate- ayā juhūḥ sā parṇamayī' iti ।
vākyaṃ ca prakṛtivikṛtyostulyameva pravartate ।
ubhayatrā'śrayabhūtāyā juhvāḥ satvāt ।
tasmāt- prakṛtivikṛtyorūmayorapyayaṃ vidhiḥ- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- kimayaṃ vidhirvikṛtau codakātpūrve niviśate, paścādvā ।
nā'dyaḥ ।
āśrayabhūtāyā juhvāścodakamantareṇāsaṃbhavāt ।
dvitīye tu parṇatvamapi juhvā sahaiva codakenātidiśyate ।
tatra punarvidhivaiyarthyādayaṃ vidhiḥ prakṛtimātragaḥ ।
evaṃ ayasya svādiraḥ strubo bhavati' ityudāharaṇīyam ।
prakaraṇaviśeṣāt tu vikṛtau virodhi syāt ।

-
dvitīyādhikaraṇamāracayati-
sāmidhenīḥ saptadaśa prakṛtau vikṛtāvuta ।
pūrvavatprakṛtau pāñcadaśyenaitadvikalpyate ।
vikṛtau sāptadaśyaṃ syātprakṛtau prakriyābalāt ।
pāñcadaśyāvaruddhatvādākāṅkṣāyā nivṛttitaḥ ।

anārabhya śrūyate- asaptadaśa sāmidhenīranubrūyāt' iti ।
apravo vājā abhidyava' - ityādyā agnisamindhanārthā ṛcaḥ sāmidhenyaḥ ।
tāsāṃ sāptadaśyaṃ pūrvabhyāyena prakṛtigatam ।
yadi prakṛtau apañcadaśa sāmidhenīranvāha' iti vidhiḥ syāt, tarhi pāñcadaśyasāptadaśye vikalpeyātām- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- vikṛtāveva sāptadaśyaṃ niviśate ।
prakṛtau pāñcadaśyenāvaruddhānāṃ sāmidhenīnāṃ saṃkhyākāṅkṣāyā abhāvāt ।
na ca - prāñcadaśyasāptadaśyavākyayoḥ samānabalatvādavarodhā bhāvaḥ- iti śaṅkanīyam ।
pāñcadaśye prakaraṇānugrahasyādhikatvāt ।
tasmāt- mitravindādhvara kalpādivikṛtau sāptadaśyamavatiṣṭhate ।
na cātra pūrvanyāyo asti ।
sāptadaśyasya codakaprāptyabhāvena punarvidhāne doṣābhāvāt ।
naimittikaṃ tu prakṛtau tadvikāraḥ saṃyogaviśeṣāt ।

-
tṛtīyādhikaraṇamāracayati-
sāptadaśyaṃ tu vaiśyasya vikṛtau prakṛtāvuta ।
pūrvavaccenna saṃkocānnitye naimittikoktitaḥ ।
godohanena praṇayetkāmītyetadudāharat ।
bhāṣyakārastadapyastu nyāyasyātra samatvataḥ ।

asaptadaśānubrūyādvaiśyasya' iti vihitaṃ vaiśyanimittaṃ sāptadaśyaṃ pūrvanyāyena vikṛtigatam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
naimittikenānena vacanena prakṛtigatasya nityasya pāñcadaśyasya vaiśyavyatirikta viṣayatayā saṃkocanīyatvāt ।
nityaṃ sāmānyarūpatayā sāvakāśatvena ca durbalam ।
naimittikaṃ tu viśeṣarūpatvaniravakāśatvābhyāṃ prabalam ।
tasmāt- vaiśyanimittakaṃ sāptadaśyaṃ prakṛtāvavatiṣṭhate ।
atra bhāṣyakāro anyadudājahāra- acamasenāpaḥ praṇayevgodohanena paśukāmasya' iti ।
tatra- prakṛteścamasenāvaruddhatvādgodohanaṃ vikṛtau- iti pūrvapakṣaḥ ।
kāmanānimittakena godohanena nityasya camasasya niṣkāmaviṣayatayā saṃkocanīyatvātprakṛtāveva godohanam- iti rāddhāntaḥ ।
iṣṭyartham agnyādheyaṃ prakaraṇāt ।
na vā tāsāṃ tadarthatvāt ।
liṅgadarśanāc ca ।

-
caturthādhikaraṇamāracayati -
ādhānaṃ pavamānāderiṣṭeraṅgaṃ na vā bhavet ।
agnīnāmiṣṭiśeṣatvāttaddvārāsya tadaṅgatā ।
anārabhya vidhāmāttu nāṅgaṃ kasyacidāhitiḥ ।
agnyarthatvāttatsameṣṭiragnayastvagnihotragāḥ ।

idamāmnāyate- aagnaye pavamānāyāṣṭādaśakapālaṃ nirvapat, agnaye pāvakāya, agnaye śucaye' iti ।
avasante brāhmaṇo agnīnādadhīta' iti ca ।
tatra- ādhānaṃ pavamānādīṣṭīnāmaṅgaṃ bhavet ।
kutaḥ ।
darśapūrṇamāsavikṛtiṣu pavamānādīṣṭiṣu codakaprāptānāmāhavamanīyādyagnīnāmiṣṭyaṅgatve satyagnidvārā tatsaṃskārarūpasyā'dhānasyāpi tadaṅgatāyā anivāryatvāt - iti cet ।
maivam ।
na hyetadādhānaṃ kasyacitkratoḥ prakaraṇe paṭhitam ।
kiṃtu - anārabhyādhītam ।
ato na kasyāpyetadaṅgam, kiṃtvādhānavadiṣṭīnāmapyagnisaṃskārārthatvātparasparaṃ nāstyaṅgāṅgibhāvaśaṅkā ।
nanu- pavamāneṣṭhyaṅgatvābhāve agnisaṃskāravaiyarthyādagnidvārā tadaṅgatvaṃ yuktam- iti cet ।
na ।
saṃskṛnāmagnīnāmagnihotrādyuttarakratuṣu tattadvākyairviniyogāvagamāt ।
tasmāt- nā'dhānamaṅgam ।
tatprakṛtyarthaṃ yathānye anārabhyavādāḥ ।
sarvārthaṃ vādhānasya svakālatvāt ।

-
pañcamādhikaraṇamāracayati -
ādhānaṃ kiṃ prakṛtyarthe vahnimātreṇa vā yutam ।
saṃskṛtāgnipranāḍyaitatparṇavatprakṛtau sthitam ।
laukikākāramātratve viphalatvātkratau yutiḥ ।
parṇasyā'havanīyādau śāstrīye astu svatantratā ।

anārabhyādhītaṃ parṇamayītvaṃ yathā juhūpranāḍyā prakṛtau niviṣṭam, tathaivāgnipranāḍyā tatsaṃskārarūpamādhānaṃ prakṛtau niviśate- iti cet ।
maivam ।
vaiṣamyāt ।
dvividho hi juhvā ākāraḥ- laukikaḥ śāstrīyaśca ।
aratnimātradairghya hasamukhatvatvagbilatvādirūpo dṛśyamāno laukikaḥ ।
apūrvīyatvākārastu śāstrīyaḥ ।
tayorapūrvīyatvaṃ kratupraveśamantareṇa nāsti ।
tatra yadi laukikākāramātre paryavasyati, tadā parṇamayītvaṃ viphalaṃ bhavet ।
kāṣṭhāntareṇāpi tadākārasya susaṃpādatvāt ।
aco apūrvīyatvāya parṇaḥ kratau praviṣṭaḥ ।
āhavanīyādīnāṃ tveka eva śāstrīyākāraḥ ।
sa ca viṅibalādādhānenaiva janyate, nānyathā ।
tasmādādhānasya kratupraveśaṃ vinaiva śāstrīvāhavanīyādyākārasaṃpādanasamartha tvādagnihotreṇa tatsaṃyujyate ।
tathā sati parṇavaiṣamyātprakṛtāvapraviśyāgnīnutpādya kratuvatsvāta tryeṇāvatiṣṭhate ।
tato laukikopāyasaṃpāditasuvarṇavrīhyādivadādhānasaṃpāditānāṃ svatantrāṇā mevā'havanīyādyagnīnāṃ paścādvākyaiḥ kratuṣu viniyogo astu ।
tāsām agniḥ prakṛtitaḥ prayājavat syāt ।
na vā tāsāṃ tadarthatvāt ।

-
ṣaṣṭhādhikaraṇamāracayati-
saṃskṛte pavamāneṣṭyā vahnau seṣṭirna veṣṭayaḥ ।
vahnau tatsaṃskṛte kāryāścodakasyānurodhataḥ ।
codakaḥ pavamāneṣṭau na tāṃ prāpayituṃ prabhuḥ ।
anaṅgatveṣṭyasiddhibhyāmiṣṭayasyadasaṃskṛte ।

pāvamānādīṣṭibhirāhavanīyādyagnayaḥ saṃskriyante ।
saṃskṛteṣvagniṣvagnihotradarśapūrṇamāsādi kratavaḥpravartante ।
tathā sati- vimatāḥ pavamāneṣṭayastābhiriṣṭibhiḥ saṃskṛte bahnau kartavyāḥ, iṣṭitvāt, itareṣṭivat ।
codako apyevaṃ ।
satyanugṛhīto bhavati ।
etābhiriṣṭibhiḥ saṃskṛte bahnau prakṛtyanuṣṭhānāt- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- yadyapi pavamāneṣṭirvikṛtiḥ, tathāpi codako na tasyāṃ pavamāneṣṭau pavamāneṣṭi matideṣṭuṃ prabhavati ।
prakṛtau prayājādivatpavamāneṣṭeraṅgatvābhāvāt ।
kiṃca- aetasyāḥ pavamāneṣṭeḥ saṃskṛtāgnisiddhyartha pavamāneṣṭyantarāṅgīkāre tatrāpi tathā' ityanavasthāyāmiṣṭireva na sidhyet ।
tasmāt- tābhiriṣṭibhirasaṃskṛte vahnau pavamāneṣṭayaḥ kartavyāḥ ।
tulyaḥ sarveṣāṃ paśuvidhiḥ prakaraṇāviśeṣāt ।
sthānāc ca pūrvasya ।
śvas tv ekeṣāṃ tatra prākśrutir guṇārthā ।
tenotkṛṣṭasya kālavidhir iti cet ।
naikadeśatvāt ।
artheneti cet ।
na śrutivipratiṣedhāt ।
sthānāt tu pūrvasya saṃskārasya tadarthatvāt ।
liṅgadarśanāc ca ।
acodanā vā guṇārthena ।

-
saptamādhikaraṇamāracayati -
agnīṣomīyasavanīyānubandhyapaśuṣvamī ।
upākaraṇamukhyāstu dharmāḥ sādhāraṇa na vā ।
jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe pāṭhātsādhāraṇa amī ।
paśudharmāgrahātsomayāge te syurnirarthakāḥ ।
agnīṣomīyadharmatvaṃ teṣāṃ sthānātprasidhyati ।
dvayoritarayoḥ paśrvoḥ prāpyante codakena te ।

agnīṣomīyaḥ, savanīyaḥ, anubandhyaśca, ityete trayaḥ paśavo jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇe samāmnātāḥ ।
paśudharmāścopākaraṇaparyagnikaraṇādayastatrā'mnātāḥ ।
aprajāpaterjāyamānāḥ' aimaṃ paśum'- ityābhyāmṛgbhyāṃ paśorupasparśanamupākaraṇam ।
darbhajvālayā triḥ pradakṣiṇīkaraṇaṃ paryagnikaraṇam ।
ta ete dharmāstriṣvapi paśuṣu sādhāraṇyena vidhīyante ।
trayāṇāmapi jyotiṣṭomaprakaraṇapāṭhasāmyāt ।
nanu jyotiṣṭhomasya prakaraṇe paṭhitānetāndharmānsa eva grahīṣyati, na tu paśavaḥ- iti cet ।
na ।
tasya somayāgatvāt ।
somo hyabhiṣavādīndharmānākā ṅkṣati, na tu yūpaniyojanaviśasanādīn ।
tasmāt- aṅginyanarthakāḥ santo aṅgeṣu niviśamānā aviśeṣatastriṣvapi paśuṣvavatiṣṭhante- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- astyatra viśeṣaḥ saṃnidhilakṣaṇaḥ ।
sautyanāmakādahnaḥ prācīna aupavasathyanāmake ahni dhiṣṇyanirmāṇādūrdhvamete dharmā āmnātāḥ ।
agnīṣomīyasyāpi tadeva sthānam ।
savanīyastu sautye ahani śrūyate- aāśvinaṃ grahaṃ gṛhītvā trivṛtā yūpaṃ parivīyā'gneyaṃ savanīyaṃ paśumupākaroti' iti ।
anubandhyastvavabhṛthānte samāmnātaḥ ।
tataḥ saṃnidhinā te dharmā agnīṣomīye saṃbadhyante, savanīyānubandhyayostu codakādatidiśyante ।
dohayoḥ kālabhedād asaṃyuktaṃ śṛtaṃ syāt ।
prakaraṇavibhāgād vā tatsaṃyuktasya kālaśāstram ।

-
aṣṭamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
śākhāchedādayo dohe dharmāḥ sāyaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ।
prātaśca santi vā sāyaṃ sthānātte pūrvavatsthitāḥ ।
ānarthakyapratihatiḥ pūrvavanneha vidyate ।
balino ataḥ prakaraṇātprātardohe api santi te ।

darśapūrṇamāsaṃprakaraṇe - palāśaśākhāchedanam, tayā śākhayā vatsāpākaraṇam, ityādayo dohadharmāḥ samāmnātāḥ ।
dohau ca dvau vidyete-amāvāsyāyāṃ rātrāveko dohaḥ ।
pratipadi prātaraparo dohaḥ ।
tatra pūrvanyāyena prāthamike sāyaṃdohe prathamaśrutāste dharmā vyavatiṣṭhante- iti cet ।
maivam ।
veṣamyāt ।
pūrvatra hi some viśasanādidharmāṇāmananvayātprakaraṇamānarthakyaprati hatam ।
iha tu nāstyānarthakyapratihatiḥ ।
tataḥ prakaraṇena sthānaṃ bādhitvā dvayordohayoste dharmā abhyupeyāḥ ।
tadvat savanāntare grahāmnānam ।

navamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
grahadharmāḥ sādanādyāḥ prātaḥsavana eva te ।
triṣu vā niścitasthānādādyaḥ pūrvavaduttaraḥ ।

jyotiṣṭome prātaḥsavane santyaindravāyavādayo grahāḥ, mādhyaṃdine savane marutvatīyādayaḥ, tṛtīyasavana ādityādayaḥ ।
tatra sādanasaṃmārgādayo dharmāḥ prātaḥsavanīyagrahasaṃnidhāvāmnāyante - aupopte anye grahāḥ sādyante, anupopte dhruvaḥ' iti ।
adaśāpavitreṇa grahaṃ saṃmārṣṭi' iti ca ।
dhruvavyatiriktānāṃ grahāṇāmadhastānmṛttikopaveśanaṃ kṛtvā tatra sādanam, dhruvasya tu na tathā ।
pūrvādhikaraṇe śāśāharaṇādayaḥ pradhānayordadhipayasorrdhamāḥ samāmnātāḥ ।
tacca dadhi pūrvodyuḥ sāyaṃdohamantareṇa na sidhyatīti tatsiddhyarthe kevalaṃ sāyaṃ duhyate, na tu sāyaṃdohasyāsādhāraṇa tvena dharmaiḥ sahaikasmindeśe pāṭho astīti sthānaṃ na niścitam, iha tu tanniścitamiti prātaḥsavana eva te dharmā iti cet ।
maivam ।
sādanādīnāṃ vākyena grahadharmatvaṃ, prakaraṇena jyotiṣṭomadharmatvaṃ cāvagamyate ।
tasminniścitamapi sthānaṃ vākyaprakaraṇābhyāṃ bādhitvā triṣu sabaneṣu sādanādayo avatiṣṭhante ।
raśanā ca liṅgadarśanāt ।
daśamādhikaraṇamāracayati-

-
ekatraivota sarvatra raśanāveṣṭanādayaḥ ।
agnīṣomīya evaite kramālliṅgādito antimaḥ ।

agnīṣomīyapaśusaṃnidhau raśanayā yūpasya veṣṭanam, raśanāyāstrivṛttvaṃ darbhamayatvaṃ ca, ityādayo dharmā āmnātāḥ- aparivyayati, ūrgvai raśanā' iti, atriṣṛdbhavati' iti, adarbhamayī bhaviti' iti ca ।
tatra yeyaṃ raśanā, ye ca veṣṭanādayaḥ, te sarve saṃnidheravāntaraprakaraṇā dvāgnīṣomīya eva syuḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
savanīyapaśāvapi tatsadbhāvo liṅgādavagamyate ।
atrivṛtā yūpaṃ parinīyā'gneyaṃ savanīyaṃ paśumupākaroti' iti trivṛttvaparivyāṇayoḥ siddhavadanuvādoliṅgam ।
kiṃca tṛtīyāśrutyā vākyena ca parivyāṇasya yūpadharmatā, na tu paśudharmatā ।
yūpaśca trayāṇāṃ paśūnāṃ tantram, iti vakṣyate ।
tasmāt- sarveṣu paśudhvete dharmāḥ syuḥ ।
ārāc chiṣṭam asaṃyuktam itaraiḥ saṃnidhānāt ।
saṃyuktaṃ vā tadarthatvāc cheṣasya tannimittatvāt ।
nirdeśād vyavatiṣṭheta ।

ekādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
grahadharmā anārabhyoktāṃśvadābhyadvayena hi ।
vidyante vā prakaraṇādādyo vākyādihāntimaḥ ।

anārabhya dvau grahau śrutau- aaṃśuṃ gṛhṇāti' iti, aadābhyaṃ gṛhṇāti' iti ca ।
tayoḥ sādanasaṃmārgādayo grahadharmā na vidyante ।
kutaḥ ।
ārabhyādhīteṣvaindravāyavādiṣveva prakaraṇena vyavasthāpitatvāt - iti cet ।
maivam ।
agrahāḥ sādyante' ityādivākyena grahadharmatvāvagame tayorapi grahayoranivārya tvāt ।
na caindravāyavādayaḥ prakaraṇinaḥ ।
jyotiṣṭhomo hi prakaraṇī ।
tasmātsanti tayorrdhamāḥ ।
agnyaṅgam aprakaraṇe tadvat ।

-
dvādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
akhaṇḍādīṣṭakādharmāścitriṇyādiṣu nocitāḥ ।
santi vā vākyamapyatrānārabhyoktaṃ tato na te ।
prakṛtāpūrvasaṃbandhāttādṛśādapi vākyataḥ ।
akhaṇḍatvādayo agnyarthacitriṇyādiṣu santi te ।

anārabhya śrūyate- acitriṇīrupadadhāti' iti ।
agniprakaraṇe ceṣṭakānāṃ dharmāḥ śrutāḥ- aakhaṇḍāmakṛṣṇāṃ kuryāt' iti ।
pūrvatra- aṃśvadābhyayorutpattivākyasyānārabhyādhītatve api viniyojakavākyaṃ prakaraṇādhītam ।
citriṇyādināmakānāṃ tviṣṭakāviśeṣāṇāṃ viniyojakaṃ vākyamapyanārabhyāghītam ।
tacca cityantare tāścitriṇīrviniyuṅkte ।
akhaṇḍatvādidharmāstu ṣaṇṇāṃ citīnāṃ madhye prathamacitāvāmnātāḥ ।
tasmāt- te citriṇyādiṣu nocitāḥ- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- yadyapyutpattiviniyojakavākyayoranyatarasyāpi prakaraṇapāṭho nāsti, tathāpi aya evaṃ vidvānagniṃ cinute' iti prakṛtaṃ yadetadagnyapūrve tatsaṃbandhitvenaivacitriṇyādayo apyaprakaraṇa paṭhitenāpi vākyena viniyujyante ।
akhaṇḍatvādayañcāgnisādhanabhūteṣṭakādharmāḥ, na tu prathamaciti dharmāḥ ।
tasmāt- agnisādhanabhūtāsu citriṇyādīṣṭakāsvapi te santi ।
naimittikam atulyatvād asamānavidhānaṃ syāt ।

-
trayodaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
vidhayo abhiṣavādyāḥ syuḥ phalākhye camase na vā ।
naimittikasya nityena tulyatvādasti tadvidhiḥ ।
nitye kṛtārthāḥ saṃskārāḥ paścādbhāvinimittaje ।
na vidheyāḥ kiṃtu tatra prāpyantāmatideśataḥ ।

nyagrodhamukularūpasya phalasya piṣṭaṃ camyate yatra sa phalacamasaḥ ।
sa ca naimittikaḥ ।
rājanyavaiśyau nimittīkṛtya vihitatvāt ।
somastu nityaḥ ।
upādhikramamapyanupajīvyaiva asomena yajeta' iti vihitatvāt ।
tasya ca nitvasya somasya yathā yāgasādhanatvam, tathā phalacamasasyāpi tadasti ।
tasmāt asomamabhipuṇoti' asomaṃ krīṇāti' ityādayo yāgadravya saṃskāravidhayaḥ soma iva phalacamase api pravartante- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- nityā abhikvādisaṃskārā nityaṃ somaṃ saṃskārya labdhvā caritārthāḥ santo nānyaṃ saṃskāryamapekṣante ।
phalacamasastu soyavikāratvātpaścādbhāvī ।
tato nirapekṣāḥ saṃskāravidhayo na tatra pravartante ।
na caitāvatā saṃskārābhāvaḥ ।
codakena tatsiddhaḥ ।
tasmāt- somamātrasaṃbandhino vidhayaḥ ।
pratinidhiś ca tadvat ।
tadvatprayojanaikatvāt ।
aśāstralakṣaṇatvācca ।

caturdaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
nīvārādipratinidheratulyo vā vidhiḥ samaḥ ।
purevātulyatā sāmyamākārādbrīhitā yataḥ ।

avrīhibhiryajeta' iti vihitānāṃ vrīhīṇāmasaṃbhave nībārāḥ pratinidhitvena svīkāryā iti vakṣyate ।
tatra pūrvanyāyenāvaghātādividhayo vrīhiṣu kṛtārthāḥ paścādbhāvini nīvārādau na pravartante- iti cet ।
maivam ।
vrīhiśabdo hi jātiviśeṣeṇā'kāraviśeṣeṇa vopetaṃ dravyamācaṣṭe ।
nīvāreṣu jātito vrīhiśabdārthatvābhāve apyākārato vrīhiśabdārthatvena avrīhīnavahanti' iti vidhiḥ pravartate ।
yathā vrīhijātāveva samīcīnānāṃ vrīhīṇāmabhāve jalavahnyādyupaghātena sāravikaleṣvapi vidhiḥ, tathā jātivikaleṣvapi brīhiṣu mukhyaikadeśarūpatvādvidhirastu ।
niyamārthā guṇaśrutiḥ ।

pañcadaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
pūtīkābhiṣavo atulyastulyo vā somatulyatā ।
nāsti naimittikatvena tulyaḥ pratinidhitvataḥ ।

ayadi somaṃ na vindeta, pūti kānabhiṣuṇuyāt' iti śrūyate ।
tatra somābhāvaṃ nimittīkṛtya pūtīkalatākhaṇḍānāṃ vihitatvātphalacamasavannaimittikatvena somābhiṣavakrayādividhiḥ pūtīkeṣu na tulyaḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
nīvārabatpratinidhitvāt ।
nanu- pratinidhitve svayamevopāditsitatvādvidhirnāpekṣitaḥ ।
ata eva nīvāreṣu vidhirna śrutaḥ- iti cet ।
na ।
vidherniyamārthatvasya ṣaṣṭhe vakṣyamāṇatvāt ।
tasmāt- abhiṣavakrayādividhiḥ somapūtīkayostulyaḥ ।
saṃsthās tu samānavidhānāḥ prakaraṇāviśeṣāt ।
vyapadeśaś ca tulyavat ।
vikārās tu kāmasaṃyoge nityasya samatvāt ।
api vā dviruktatvāt prakṛter bhaviṣyantīti ।
vacanāt tu samuccayaḥ ।
pratiṣedhāc ca pūrvaliṅgānām ।
guṇaviśeṣād ekasya vyapadeśaḥ ।

-
ṣoḍaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
ukthyādiṣu samo dīkṣaṇīyādyaṅgavidhirna vā ।
ekaprakaraṇatvena phalavattvācca tulyatā ।
ukthyādayaḥ kāmayogādvikārāḥ prakriyā tataḥ ।
agniṣṭomātmake jyotiṣṭomamātre ca tadvidhiḥ ।

jyotiṣṭomaḥ- svayameko api samāptibhedādbhidyate ।
yajñāyajñiyastotreṇa samāptau aagniṣṭomaḥ' ityucyate ।
tasmādapi stotrādūrdhvamukthyastotreṇa samāptau aukthyaḥ' ityucyate ।
evaṃ ṣoḍaśyādayo api ।
tādṛśasya saptasaṃsthāvato jyotiṣṭomasya prakaraṇe dīkṣaṇīyeṣṭiprāyaṇīyeṣṭyādīnāmaṅgānāṃ vidhirāmnātaḥ ।
sa ca vidhirjyotiṣṭomasya prathamasaṃsthāviśeṣe agniṣṭome yathā pravṛttaḥ, tathaivokthyādiṣvapi pravartate ।
kutaḥ ।
prakaraṇasaṃbandhasya samānatvāt ।
kiṃca- yathāgniṣṭomaḥ phalatvādaṅgavidhibhiḥ saṃyujyate, evamukthyādayo api ।
teṣāṃ ca phalamevamāmnāyate-'paśukāma ukthyaṃ gṛhṇīyāt' aṣoḍaśinā vīryakāmaḥ stuvīta' aatirātreṇa prajākāmaṃ yājayet' iti ।
tasmāt - saptasvapi saṃsthāsu samāno aṅgavidhiḥ- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- yadetadukthyādīnāṃ phalamudāhṛtam, tattu teṣāṃ vikāratvaṃ gamayati ।
akāmyo guṇaḥ śrūyamāṇo nityamartha vikṛtya niviśate' iti nyāyādyathā godohanaguṇo nityaṃ camasasādhanakamapāṃ praṇayanaṃ vikṛtya niviśate,evamukthyaguṇo nityāmagniṣṭomasya saṃsthāṃ vikṛtya saṃsthāntaratvaṃ gamayati ।
tato agniṣṭomasya guṇavikārā ukthyādaya iti na sarvasaṃsthāsādhāraṇaṃ prakaraṇam, kiṃtu - agniṣṭomasyai vāsādhāraṇama ।
nanu- ajyotiṣṭomena yajeta' ityuktatvājjyotiṣṭomasyedaṃ prakaraṇam, na tvagniṣṭomasaṃsthāyāḥ- iti cet ।
bāḍham ।
asā jyotiṣṭomo na kadācidapyagniṣṭomaṃ vyabhicarati ।
ukthyādīnāmapyantarbhāvitāgniṣṭomakatvāt ।
ukthyādīṃstu vyabhicarati ।
vināpi tairagniṣṭomaśśāyāṃ jyotiṣṭomatvasaṃbhavāt ।
ato agniṣṭomasaṃsthasya jyotiṣṭomasyedaṃ prakaraṇaṃ sattatraiva dīkṣaṇīyādyaṅgavidhiṃ niveśayati ।
ukthyādiṣu codakādaṅgānyatidiśyante ।
iti śrīmādhavīye jauminīyanyāyamālāvistare tṛtīyādhyāyasya ṣaṣṭha pādaḥ

atha tṛtīyādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pādaḥ ।
prakaraṇaviśeṣād asaṃyuktaṃ pradhānasya ।
sarveṣāṃ vā śeṣatvasyātatprayuktatvāt ।
ārādapīti cet ।
na tadvākyaṃ hi tadarthatvāt ।
liṅgadarśanāc ca ।
saptamapādasya prathamādhikaraṇamāracayati -

-
mukhyāṅgataiva vedyādeḥ prayājādyaṅgato api vā ।
tadvākyaṃ prakriyāyuktaṃ mukhyāṅgatvasya bodhakam ।
mukhyāṅgasyāpi vedyādeḥ prayājādiṣu cāṅgatā ।
mukhyārthatvātprayājādeḥ svāpūrvavyavadhānataḥ ।

darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate- avedyāṃ havīṃṣyāsādayati' abarhiṣi havīṃṣyāsādayati' iti ।
tathā taddharmāḥ śrūyante- avediṃ khanati' abarhirlunāti' ityādayaḥ ।
mukhyahavīṃṣyāgneyapuroḍāśādīni, amukhyahavīṃṣi tu prayājādyarthāni ।
tatra-svasvadharmasahitāni vedyādīni prakaraṇabalānmukhyahaviṣā mevāṅgāni- avedyāṃ havīṃṣyāsādayati' iti vākyātsarvahaviraṅgatā- iti cet ।
na ।
prakaraṇena vākyasya saṃkocanīyatvāt ।
yadi vākyaṃ prakaraṇanairapekṣyeṇa svatantraṃ syāt, tadā sādanamātraparyavasānena yāgābhāve vaiyarthya syāt ।
saumikahīvaṣāmapyetadvedyāsādanaṃ prasajyeta ।
tasmāt- mukhyahaviraṅgaṃ vedyādikam- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- astu vaiyarthyātiprasaṅgaparihāreṇa prakṛtāpūrvasādhanabhūtahaviḥṣu vedyāderaṅgatvam ।
prayājādihavīṃṣyapi svakīyāvāntarāpūrvadvārā mukhyāpūrvasādhanānyeveti tadaṅgatvamapi vedyāderyuktam ।
evaṃ sati vākyasyātyantasaṃkoco na bhaviṣyati ।
phalasaṃyogāt tu svāmiyuktaṃ pradhānasya ।
dvitīyādhikaraṇamāracayati-
vapanādyupakāraḥ kiṃ dvayormukhāṅgayoruta ।
mukhya eva dvayorastu kṛtsnakartṛgatatvataḥ ।
yuktaḥ śāstrīyasaṃskāro mukhyasya phalabhojinaḥ ।
vināpi saṃsakṛtiṃ dṛṣṭaṃ kartṛtvaṃ tatra nāsti saḥ ।

jyotiṣṭome keśaśmaśruvapanapayovratādayo yajamānasaṃskārā āmnātāḥ ।
grahaiḥ somahomo jyotiṣṭome mukhyaḥ ।
agnīṣomīyapaśvādikamaṅgam ।
tatra-dvayormukhyāṅgayorete vapanādaya upakurvanti ।
kutaḥ ।
kartṛdharmatvāt ।
yajamāno hi kartṛtayā vapanādibhiḥ saṃskriyate ।
kartṛtvaṃ ca yathā mukhyaṃ prati tasya vidyate, tathāṅgaṃ pratyapyasti ।
tasmāt-ubhayorupakāraḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
dvau hi yajamānasyā'kārau- kriyākartṛtvam, phalabhoktṛtvaṃ ceti ।
tayoradṛṣṭaḥ phalabhogaḥ, kriyāniṣpattiśca dṛṣṭā ।
tathā sati- vapanādikṛtopakāratyāpyadṛṣṭatvādbhoktṛśeṣā vapanādayaḥ phalabhogasādhane mukhya eva paryavasyanti ।
vapanādisaṃskārarahitairapyṛtvigbhiḥ kṛṣīvalādibhiśca kriyā niṣpādyamānā dṛśyate ।
tatastatra kartṛtvākāre vapanādikṛtaḥ sa upakāro nāsti ।
tasmāt-adṛṣṭa phalabhojino asya yajamānasya yo ayamadṛṣṭarūpaḥ śāstrīyaḥ saṃskāraḥ so ayaṃ mukhye karmaṇi yukto nāṅgeṣu ।
nātra pūrvavadvākyamasti, yena paramparāphalasādhaneṣvaṅgeṣu vapanādyupakāraḥ śaṅkayeta ।
prakaraṇaṃ tu mukhyasyaiva, na tvaṅgānām ।
tasmāt- na teṣūpakāraḥ ।
cikīrṣayā ca saṃyogāt ।
tadyukte tu phalaśrutis tasmāt sarvacikīrṣā syāt ।

-
tṛtīyādhikaraṇamāracayati-
mukhyārthā saumikī vedirubhayārthota mukhyagā ।
cikīrṣitatvānmukhyasya vedyā tatkṛtisaṃbhavāt ।
mukhyapauṣkalyahetutvāttadaṅgaṃ ca cikīrṣitam ।
mukhyavattena tadvediraṅgeṣvapyupakāriṇī ।

dārśikīṃ vediṃ madhye antarbhāvya prācīnavaṃśo maṇḍapo avasthitaḥ ।
tataḥ pūrvasyāṃ diśi sadohavirdhānādīnāṃ paryāpto bhūbhāgaviśeṣaḥ ।
taiḥ sadaḥprabhṛtibhiḥ saha saumikī vedirityucyate ।
seyaṃ mukhyasya somayāgasyaivopakāraṃ karoti, na tvamukhyānāmagnīṣomīyādyaṅgānām ।
kutaḥ ।
mukhyasya cikīrṣitatvāt ।
na ca - aṅgānyapi cikīrṣitāni- iti vācyam ।
cikīrṣāsvarūpasya vedenaivābhihitatvāt ।
evaṃ śrūyate- aṣaṭtriṃśatprakramā prācī, caturviṃśatiragreṇa, triṃśajjaghanena, iyati śakṣyāmahe' iti ।
asyāyamarthaḥ- śrūyamāṇenānena dairdhyapramāṇena tiryakpramāṇadvayena ca pramite bhūbhāge phalahetusomayāgaṃ kartu śakṣyāmahe' iti niścitya tathaiva kuryāta- iti ।
seyaṃ cikīrṣā mukhyaviṣayā ।
aiyati śakṣyāmahe' iti parimāṇasya śakteścopanyāsāt ।
aṅgānāṃ tu paśūnāmiṣṭīnāṃ ca sadohavirdhānādi maṇṭapanirapekṣāṇāṃ yathoktaparimāṇamantareṇāpyanuṣṭhātuṃ śakyatvātsa upanyāsastatra nirarthakaḥ ।
somasya tvanuṣṭhānaṃ yathoktavedyāmeva saṃbhavati, natvanyatra ।
tasmāt- sā vedirmukhyasyaivopakaroti- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- aiyati śakṣyāmahe' ityatra sāṅgapradhānānuṣṭhāne śaktiruktā ।
tādṛśasyaiva phalaṃ prati puṣkalahetutvāt ।
ato mukhyāṅgayościkīrṣāyāstulyatvādvedirubhayārthā ।
na ca- atra vapanādisāmyaṃ śaṅkanīyam ।
dṛṣṭopayogābhāvasya tatroktatvāt ।
iha tu- havirāsādanādirdṛṣṭa upayogaḥ ।
sa ca mukhyāṅgayoḥ sama ityubhayārthatvam ।
tathābhidhānena ।
guṇābhidhānāt sarvārtham abhidhānam ।

-
caturthādhikaraṇamāracayati-
caturhotrā paurṇamāsīṃ mṛśedājyādimarśane ।
mantro mukhya utāṅge api mukhye tadvāciśabdataḥ ।
śabdasya karmavācitvāttatra marśanavarjanāt ।
vibhaktivyatyaye mantro mukhyāṅgahaviṣordvayoḥ ।

darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ śrūyate- acaturhotrā paurṇamāsīmabhimṛśet, pañcahotrābhāvāsyām' iti ।
pṛthivī hotā'- ityādiko mantraścaturhotā ।
tasminmantre yajñāṅgānāṃ caturṇā śrutatvāt ।
athavā- tasya mantrasyābhimānitvenā'tmabhūtaḥ kaścitpuruṣaḥ prajāpatinā caturthāramāmantritaḥ pratvuttaramuvāceti sa puruṣaścaturhūtaḥ ।
tadīyanāmnā mantro api acaturhūtaḥ' ityucyate ।
apūjyānāṃ pratyakṣanāmagrahaṇamayuktam' ityabhiprāyeṇa hūtaśabdasthāne hotṛśabdaḥ paṭhyate ।
ayamarthaḥ sarvo api taittirīyabrāhmaṇe śrūyate-
"ātmannātmannityāmantrayata ।
tasmai caturhūtaḥ pratyaśṛṇot ।
sa caturhūto abhavat ।
caturhūto ha vai nāmaiṣaḥ ।
taṃ vā etaṃ caturhūtaṃ santaṃ acaturhotā' ityācakṣate parokṣeṇa ।
parokṣapriyā iva hi devaḥ"iti ।
aagnirhotā'- ityādiko mantraḥ pañcahotā ।
tatrāpyuktaprakāro draṣṭavyaḥ ।
- atra-yo ayamājyādihaviṣa upasparśanārtho mantraḥ, asau mukhya eva haviṣi niviśate ।
paurṇamāsyamāvāsyāśabdayormukhyahavirviṣaya tvāt-iti prāpte,-
brūmaḥ- paurṇamāsyabhāvāsyaśabdau karmavācinau, na tu havirvācinau ।
na ca karmaṇorupasparśana saṃbhavaḥ ।
atha kālavivakṣāyāṃ vibhaktivyatyayena saptamyartho vyākhyāyeta, tadā kālasaṃbandhasya mukhyāṅga yorubhayostulyatvādubhayavidhahavirupasparśane mantro viniyujyate ।
dīkṣādakṣiṇaṃ tu vacanāt pradhānasya ।
nivṛttidarśanāc ca ।

-
pañcamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
daṇḍadīkṣā dakṣiṇā tu śataṃ dvādaśamiryutam ।
dvayārthamuta mukhyārthe somasyetyuktisaṃbhavāt ।
mukhyāṅgadvayagaṃ maivaṃ pāramparyaviḍambanā ।
vacanasya na yuktātaḥ pradhānārthamidaṃ sthitam ।

jyotiṣṭome dīkṣādakṣiṇaṃ śrūyate- adaṇḍena dakṣiyati' iti, atasya dvādaśaśataṃ dakṣiṇā' iti ca ।
tatra dīkṣā mukhyāṅgayorupakaroti, tathā dakṣiṇāpi ।
na ca - dīkṣā somasya, dakṣiṇā somasya' iti vākye ṣaṣṭhyā mukhyasaṃbandha evāvagamyate, na tvaṅgasaṃbandhaḥ- iti vācyam ।
dīkṣādakṣiṇe somanaiva sākṣātsaṃbadhnītām, sa somaḥ punaraṅgaiḥ saṃbaddhaiti paramparayā dīkṣādakṣiṇayoraṅgairapi saṃbandho asti ।
tasmāt- ubhayārthe dīkṣādikam- iti prāpte,-
brūmaḥ- avyavahitasaṃbandha eva ṣaṣṭhyā abhidheyor'thaḥ ।
tadasaṃbhave tu - paramparāsaṃbandhaḥ kathaṃcidgṛhyate ।
iha tu tatsaṃbhavātpāramparya na yuktam ।
tasmāt- pradhānārtha dīkṣādikam ।
tathā yūpasya vediḥ ।
deśamātraṃ vā śiṣyenaikavākyatvāt ।

-
ṣaṣṭhādhikaraṇamāracayati -
antarvedi minotyardha yūpāṅgamuta lakṣayet ।
deśaṃ yūpāṅgamāvena vedibhāgo atra codyate ।
bahirvedyardhamityetadvākyaṃ bhidyeta tadvidhau ।
mīyamānasya yūpasya tāvāndeśo atra lakṣyate ।

agnīṣomīyapaśau ayūpaṃ minoti' iti prakṛtya śrūyate- aardhamantarvedi minoti, ardha bahirvedi' iti ।
ayūpaṃ sthāpayituṃ kiyadvistāravānavaṭo apekṣitaḥ' iti bubhutsāyāṃ tannirṇayāya yūpamūlasya sthaulyamaṅgulyādibhirmātavyam ।
tasya ca pīyamānasya yūpasya vedyabhyantarabhāgo alaṅgatvenaṃ vidhīyate- iti cet ।
maivam ।
yathā saṃskṛto vedyabhyantarabhāgaḥ aardhamantarvedi' ityanena vākyena vidhīyate, tadvada saṃskṛto bahirbhāgo abahirvedi'- ityanena vākyena vidhātavyaḥ ।
tato vākyaṃ bhidyeta ।
yadā tu vederabhyantarabāhyabhāgābhyāmupalakṣito asaṃskṛto' laukikadeśa evātra yūpāṅgatvena vidhīyate, na tu saṃskṛtavedibhāgaḥ ।
sāmidhenīs tad anvāhur iti havir dhānayor vacanāt sāmidhenīnām ।
deśamātraṃ vā pratyakṣaṃ hy arthakarma somasya ।
samākhyānaṃ ca tadvat ।

-
saptamādhikaraṇamāracayati -
havirdhāne sthito brūyātsāmidhenīrihāṅgatā ।
havirdhānasya tāsvāho taddeśo anena lakṣyate ।
vākyātsyādaṅgatā maivaṃ prakṛtyā paścime agnitaḥ ।
deśaḥ prāpto lāghavena lakṣyaḥ śakaṭasaṃnidhiḥ ।

jyotiṣṭome śrūyate- auta yatsunvanti sāmidhenīstadanvāhuḥ' - iti ।
havirdhānamaṇḍapagatayor dakṣiṇottarabhāgāvasthitayorhavirdhānanāmakayoḥ śakaṭayormadhye dakṣiṇaṃ śakaṭamatra yattacchabdābhyā mabhidhīyate ।
tasya samīpe somasyābhiṣavaḥ ।
auta' ityayaṃ śabdo athabdārthe vartate ।
aatha yasminhavirdhāne somamabhiṣuṇvanti, tasminsāmidhenīranubrūyuḥ' ।
aiha dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasya sāmidhenīṣvaṅgatvaṃ pratīyate ।
na cātra pūrvavadvākyabhedadoṣaḥ śaṅkyaḥ ।
akavākyatāyāḥ spaṣṭaṃ pratibhāsāt- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- sāmidhenīnāmiṣṭyaṅgatayā darśapūrṇamāsāvatra prakṛtiḥ ।
prakṛtau cā'havanīyāgneḥ paścimo deśaḥ sāmidhenīnāṃ sthānam ।
ihottaravederāhavanīyatvāttadapekṣayā havirdhānasya paścimadeśāvasthānāt ।
sa deśaścodakena prāptaḥ- iti na deśasya sāmidhenyaṅgatvaṃ vidhātavyam ।
kiṃtu dakṣiṇottarahavirdhānasamīpa deśayoraniyamena prāptau- dakṣiṇasyaiva havirdhānasya samīpadeśaḥ- iti niyantuṃ havirdhānena saṃnidhirlakṣyate ।
tathā sati niyamamātravidhānāllāghavaṃ bhavati ।
tvatpakṣe tvabhiṣavopalakṣitasya dakṣiṇasya havirdhānasyā tyantamaprāptaṃ sāmidhenyaṅgatvaṃ vidhīyata iti gauravam ।
tasmāddeśalakṣaṇā ।
śāstraphalaṃ prayoktari tallakṣaṇatvāt tasmāt svayaṃ prayoge syāt ।
utsarge tu pradhānatvāc cheṣakārī pradhānasya tasmād anyaḥ svayaṃ vā syāt ।
anyo vā syāt parikrayāmnānād vipratiṣedhāt pratyag ātmani ।

-
aṣṭamādhikaraṇamāracayati -
yajamānena kartavyaṃ nikhilaṃ tyāga eva vā ।
kartṛgāmiphalaśrutyā yujyate sarvakartṛtā ।
prayojake api kartṛtvamasti no cetkrayo vṛthā ।
kārye tena tyāgamātramṛtvijo anyatra kartṛtā ।

asvargakāmo yajeta' iti svargabhokturyāgakartuśca sāmānādhikaraṇyādekatvaṃ gamyate ।
pāṇiniśca asvaritañitaḥ kartrabhiprāye krimāphale'[pāsū ]iti sūtreṇa kriyāphalasya kartṛgāmitve satyātmanepadaṃ vidadhāti ।
ataḥ sāṅgakarmānuṣṭhānamantareṇa phalāsaṃbhavānnikhilaṃ yajamānena kartavyam- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- nikhilānuṣṭhānābhāve api prayojakatayā yajamānasya sarvakartṛtvamasti ।
aṣahūbhirhalaiḥ karṣati' ityatra tathādarśanāt ।
yadi svenaiva sarvamanuṣṭhīyeta, tadānīmṛtviṇāṃ parikrayo vṛthā syāt ।
tasmāt -yajamānena tyāgamātraṃ kāryam ।
anyatra sāṅgapradhāne krītasyartvijo anuṣṭhānam ।
tathā sati sākṣātparamparayā ca sarvakartṛtvasya yajamāne saṃbhavāttasya phalaṃ na virudhyate ।
tatrārthāt kartṛparimāṇaṃ syād aniyamo aviśeṣāt ।
api vā śrutibhedāt pratināmadheyaṃ syuḥ ।
ekasya karmabhedād iti cet ।
notpattau hi ।

navamādhikaraṇamāracayati -
na krītakartṛsaṃkhyāyā niyamo asatyasti vā na hi ।
aviśeṣādasti yāvatkārya tāvanta eva hi ।

ye yajamānena krītāḥ kartāra ṛtvijaḥ, teṣāṃ saṃkhyāviśeṣo yadyapi na śrutaḥ ।
tathāpi kāryānusāreṇa so avagantavyaḥ ।
te ca kāryaviśeṣāḥ kartṛsaṃyuktā evaṃ śrūyante- apuro adhvaryurvibhajati, pratiprasthātā manthinaṃ juhoti, neṣṭhā patnīmudānayati, unnetā camasānunnayati, prastotā prastauti, udgātodgāyati, pratihartā pratiharati, subrahmaṇyaḥ subrahmaṇyāmāhvayati, hotā prātaranuvākamanubrūte, maitrāvarūṇaḥ preṣyati, acchāvāko yajati, grāvastudgrāvastotrīyamanvāha' iti ।
evaṃ brahmabrāhmaṇācchaṃ syāgnīdhrapotṝṇāṃ caturṇā karmāṇyudāhāryāṇi ।
tasmāt-
yāvanti karyāṇi tāvanta ṛtvijo varītavyāḥ ।
camasādhvaryavaś ca tair vyapadeśāt ।

daśamādhikaraṇamāracayati -
camasādhvaryavo nānya ṛtvibhyo anye athavāgnimaḥ ।
yaugikyā saṃjñayā maivaṃ ṣaṣṭhyā tebhyo vibhedanāt ।

jyotiṣṭome śrūyate- acamasādhvaryūnvṛṇīte' iti ।
ye pūrvatra kāryānusāreṇādhvaryupramukhā ṛtvija uktāḥ, tebhyo na vyatiriktāścamasādhvaryavaḥ ।
kutaḥ ।
yaugikasaṃjñayā tadabhedapratīteḥ ।
ta thā devadatta eva pacikriyāyogātpācako bhavati, tathādhvaryupramukhā eva camasayogāccamasādhvaryavaḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
madhyataḥkāriṇāṃ camasādhvaryavaḥ, hotrakāṇāṃ, camasādhvaryava iti apaṭhyā bhedāvabhāsāt ।
madhyataḥkāriṇor'dhvayuhotrādayaḥ ।
hotrakāḥ pratiprasthātṛmautrāvaruṇādayaḥ ।
tasmādṛtvigbhyo anye ।
utpattau tu bahuśruteḥ ।

ekādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
tānvṛṇīteti bahutā nāsti vāsti grahaikyavat ।
neti cennātra vaiṣamyādutpattau bahutāśruteḥ ।

acamasādhvaryūnvṛṇīta' iti yadbahutvaṃ śrutam, tanna vivakṣitam ।
grahaikatvavaduddeśyagatatvāt- iti cet ।
maivam ।
grahavaiṣamyāt ।
agrahaṃ saṃmārṣṭi' ityetadgrahāṇāṃ notpattivākyam ।
camasādhvaryūṇāṃ tvetadevotpattivākyam ।
tatasteṣāmupādeyatvāttadgataṃ bahutvaṃ vivakṣitam ।
daśatvaṃ liṅgadarśanāt ।

dvādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
neyattāstyasti vā teṣāṃ na niyāmakavarjanāt ।
camasānāṃ daśatvena camasādhvaryavo daśa ।

spaṣṭor'thaḥ ।
śamitā ca śabdabhedāt ।
prakaraṇād votpattyasaṃyogāt ।

trayodaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
tebhyo anyaḥ śamitānanyo vānyaḥ saṃjñāpṛthaktvataḥ ।
varaṇābhāvato nānyaḥ saṃjñābhedastu yaugikaḥ ।

aśamitāra upeta na yajñam' ityasminmantre śrutāyāḥ śamitṛsaṃjñāyāḥ pṛthaktyāduktebhyo anyaḥ śamitā- iti cet ।
maivam ।
pṛthagvaraṇābhāvāt ।
saṃjñābhedastu paśusaṃjñapanayogādupapadyate ।
yadyapyayaṃ mantro adhvaryu kāṇḍe paṭhitaḥ, tathāpyadhvaryoḥ parāvṛttiśravaṇādadhvaryupuruṣāḥ pratiprasthātrādayaḥ śamitāraḥ ।
ata eva śrūyate- aparāvartate adhvaryuḥ paśoḥ saṃjñapyamānāt' iti ।
upagāś ca liṅgadarśanāt ।

caturdaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
anye syurupagātāra uditebhyo na vā yathā ।
loke atrāpi tathā maivaṃ nādhvaryuritiliṅgataḥ ।

yathā loke mukhyebhyo gāyakanāyakādibhyo anye pārśvasthā upagātāraḥ, tathātrāpi- iti cet ।
maivam ।
yadyuktebhyaḥ puruṣebhya upagātāro anye bhaveyuḥ, tadānīmadhvaryoḥ prasaktyabhāvāt anādhvaryurupagāyet' iti pratiṣedho anarthakaḥ syāt ।
tasmādukteṣveva yaugikaḥ saṃjñābhedaḥ ।
vikrayī tvanyaḥ karmaṇo acoditatvāt ।

pañcadaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
somavikrayyeka eṣu na vā varaṇavarjanāt ।
ekaḥ kratvarthatā nāsti vikrayasyeti bhidyate ।

kraya eva jyotiṣṭomāṅgatvena śrutaḥ, na vikrayaḥ ।
na cāvihitamṛtvijaḥ kurvanti ।
tasmādanyo vikretā ।
karmakāryāt sarveṣām ṛtviktvam aviśeṣāt ।
na vā parisaṃkhyānāt ।
pakṣeṇeti cet ।
na sarveṣām adhikāraḥ ।

-
ṣoḍaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
kimṛtvignāma sarveṣu samānamuta keṣucit ।
ṛtau yajanametiṣāṃ tulyamityasti nāma tat ।
saumyādhvarasya sapta syurdaśa cetyādisaṃkhyayā ।
na sarveṣāṃ samaṃ nāma keṣāṃcidyogarūḍhitaḥ ।

ṛtvikśabdasya pravṛttinimittamṛtau yajanama ।
tacca brahmādiṣviva canasādhvaryupvapyasti ।
tasmāt- sarveṣāmṛtvignāma samānam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
saṃkhyāśrutivirodhāt ।
asaumyasyādhvarasya yajñakratoḥ saptadaśartvijaḥ, iti śrūyate ।
tasmāt- yogamanatikramya śāstrīyarūḍhimapyāśritya keṣucidevaitamnānetyavagantavyam ।
niyamas tu dakṣiṇābhiḥ śrutisaṃyogāt ।
uktvā ca yajamānatvaṃ teṣāṃ dīkṣāvidhānāt ।

saptadaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
saṃkhyātā api ye kecinniyatā vāviśeṣataḥ ।
ādyo na dakṣiṇādāne dīkṣāyāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।

ye saptadaśa saṃkhyātāḥ, te brahmādiṣu camasādhvaryuṣu ca ye kecidicchayā grahītavyāḥ ।
viśeṣasyāśravaṇāt- iti cet ।
maivam ।
dakṣiṇāvākye dīkṣāvākye ca viśeṣaśravaṇāt ।
aṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadāti' ityuktvā tadviśeṣaḥ śrūyate- aagnīdhe dadāti' a brahmaṇe dadāti' ityādinā ।
dīkṣāvākyaṃ ca tatra prakaraṇe aye yajamānāsta ṛtvijaḥ' ityuktvānantarameva māmnādyate- aadhvaryurgṛhapatiṃ dīkṣayitvā brahmāṇaṃ dīkṣayati, tata udvātāram, tato hotāram, tatastaṃ pratiprasthātā dīkṣayitvārdhino dīkṣayati brāhmaṇācchaṃsinaṃ brahmaṇaḥ, prastotāramudgātuḥ, maitrāvaruṇaṃ hotuḥ ।
tatastaṃ neṣṭā dīkṣayitvā tṛtīyino dīkṣayati- agnīdhaṃ brahmaṇaḥ, pratihartāramudgātuḥ, acchāvākaṃ hotuḥ ।
tatastamunnetā dīkṣayitvā pādino dīkṣayati- potāraṃ brahmaṇaḥ, subrahmaṇyamudgātuḥ, grāvastutaṃ hotuḥ ।
tatastamanyo brāhmaṇo dīkṣayati' iti asyāyamarthaḥ- aadhvaryuryajurvedaproktaṃ karoti, tasya puruṣāstrayaḥ-brāhmaṇācchaṃsī, agnīt, potā ceti ।
udgātodgānaṃ karoti, tasya puruṣāstrayaḥ - prastotā, pratihartā, subrahmaṇyaśceti ।
hotā śaṃsanaṃ karoti, tasya puruṣāstrayaḥ- maitrāvaruṇaḥ acchāvākaḥ, grāvastuditi ।
caturṣu vargeṣu ye prathamāste dakṣiṇāṃ saṃpūrṇā prāpnuvanti ।
ye dvitīyāste tadardha prāpnuvanti- ityardhinaḥ ।
ye tṛtīyāste tṛtīyāṃśaṃ prāpnuvanti- iti tṛtīyinaḥ ।
ye caturthāste caturthamaṃśaṃ prāpnuvanti- iti pādinaḥ ।
tāmetānuktakrameṇa sa sa puruṣaḥ saṃskaroti' iti ।
atra - dīkṣāvākye nirdiṣṭā adhvaryuprabhṛtaya ṛtvijaḥ ṣoḍaśa, na tu camasādhvaryavaḥ- iti niyamo draṣṭavyaḥ ।
svāmisaptadaśāḥ karmasāmānyāt ।

aṣṭādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
sadasye yajamāne vā sāptadaśyaṃ vṛtatvataḥ ।
sadasye kurute kiṃcinnāsau svāmini tattvataḥ ।

adhvaryubrahmādiṣu ṣoḍaśasu vyavasthiteṣu saptadaśasaṃkhyāpūrakaḥ kaścidṛtvigavaikṣitaḥ ।
so atra sadasyo bhaviṣyati ।
sadasyavasthitaḥ sadasyaḥ ।
na ca tasya varaṇābhāvaḥ ।
keṣāṃcicchākhāyāṃ tadvaraṇasyā'mnātatvāt ।
tataḥ sāptadaśyaṃ sadasye paryavasitam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
asau sadasyaḥ kiṃcidapi na karoti ।
asadasya idaṃ kuryāt' iti vidhyabhāvāt ।
na ca vinā kriyāmṛtuyajananimitta ṛtvikśabdastasminnavakalpate ।
yajamānastu tyāgaṃ karotīti tasminnupapadyate ।
tasmātsāptadaśyaṃ yajamāne yuktam ।
te sarvārthāḥ prayuktatvād agnayaś ca svakālatvāt ।
tatsaṃyogāt karmaṇo vyavasthā syāt saṃyogasyārthavattvāt ।
tasyopadeśasamākhyānena nirdeśaḥ ।
tadvac ca liṅgadarśam ।

ekonaviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
na kārya niyataṃ teṣāṃ niyataṃ vāgrimo yataḥ ।
śaktāḥ kena kimityatra niyatiḥ syātsamākhyayā ।

teṣāmadhvaryuprabhṛtīnāṃ kārya na niyatam ।
yataḥ sarve sarvatra śaktāḥ ।
prakaraṇaṃ ca sarvasādhāraṇatvānna niyāmakam- iti cet-
maivam ।
samākhyāyā niyāmakatvāt ।
yasminkarmaṇi aādhvaryavam' iti samākhyā tatkarmādhvaryoḥ ।
evamitaratrāpi ।
agnayaśca svakālatvāt ।
viśādhikaraṇamāracayati-

prakṛtyartho atha sarvārtho vahnirādyo astu parṇavat ।
parṇanyāyo atidiṣṭe syādupadiṣṭe tu sarvagaḥ ।

yathā ayasya parṇamayī juhūrbhavati na sa pāpaṃ ślokaṃ śṛṇoti' ityasau parṇavidhiḥ prakṛtyarthaḥ ।
evamādhānasyāpyanārabhyā dhītatvādāhita āhavanīyādyagniḥ prakṛtyarthaḥ- iti cet-
maivam ।
vaiṣamyāt ।
parṇavākyātparṇatāyā yāvatkratupraveśe juhūrdvāram ।
sā ca juhūḥ prakṛtāveva vihitā vikṛtiṣu sarvatrātidiśyate ।
āhavanīyādyagnestu kraptupradeśe dvāraṃ homaḥ ।
sa ca kvacitprakṛtāveva vihitaḥ sanvikṛtāvatidiśyate ।
tadyathāprayāṇanāriṣṭhādihomāḥ ।
tādṛśe viṣaye ayadāhavanīye juhvati' iti vākyenāgniḥ prakṛtāveva vidhīyate ।
vikṛtau tu homena sahātidiśyate ।
tasmāsatra parṇanyāyaḥ ।
yastu homo vikṛtāvupadiśyate ।
tadyathā- sāṃgrahaṇyāmiṣṭāvāmanahomaḥ ।
tatra dvārarabhūtasya homasya vikṛtāvupadiśyamānatayā dvāriṇo api prakṛtāviva vikṛtāvapi vākyena vidhirdhārayitumaśakyaḥ ।
tasmāt- sarvārtho vahniḥ ।
praiṣānuvacanaṃ maitrāvaruṇasyopadeśāt ।
puro'nuvākyādhikāro vā praiṣasaṃnidhānāt ।
prātar anuvāke ca hotṛdarśanāt ।

-
ekaviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
yanmaitrāvaruṇaḥ preṣyatyanu cā'heti bādhanam ।
hautrādikasamākhyāyāstatsarvatrota kutracit ।
ādyo astu vacanānmaivaṃ sāhityoktyupalambhanāt ।
praiṣānuvacane yatra sahite tatra bādhanam ।

agnīṣomīyapaśau śrūyate- amaitrāvaruṇaḥ preṣyati cānu cā'ha' iti ।
tadetadvākyaṃ praiṣānuvacanayormaitrāvaruṇakartṛkatāṃ vidadhāti ।
tena ca vākyena samākhyā bādhyate ।
aagnaye samidhyamānāyānubrūhi' ayūpāyājyamānāyānubrūhi' ityādipraiṣāṇāmadhvaryu kartṛkatvadarśanāt- aādhvaryavāḥ praiṣāḥ' ityasti yājñikānāṃ samākhyā ।
tathā ।
apravo bājā abhidyavaḥ'- aañjanti tvāmadhvare devayantaḥ' ityādyanuvacanānāṃ hotṛkartṛkatvadarśanāt ।
aanuvacanāni hautrāṇi'- iti yājñikasamākhyā ।
praiṣānuvacane ca dvividhe- samaste vyaste ca ।
pūrvodāhṛte vyaste ।
ahotāpakṣadagniṃ samidham'- ityādyanuvacanamantrasyānte ahotaryaja' iti praiṣa āmnātaḥ ।
ete praiṣānuvacane samaste ।
teṣu ca vyastasamastapraiṣānuvacaneṣu sarvatra prabalena vākyena samākhyāṃ bādhitvā hotṛkartṛkatvamadhvaryukartṛkatvaṃ ca parityajya maitrāvaruṇakartṛkatvamevābhyupayem- iti prāpte-
abhidhīyate- apreṣyati cānu cā'ha' iti cakāradvayena praiṣānuvacanayoḥ samuccayo vākye asminnupalabhyate ।
tataḥ samuccitrayoreva samākhyābādhanam ।
vyastayostu yathāsamākhyaṃ hotrādikartṛkatvamevābhyupeyam ।
camasāṃścamasādhvaryavaḥ samākhyānāt ।
adhvaryur vā tannyāyatvāt ।
camase cānyadarśanāt ।
aśaktau te pratīyeran ।

-
dvāviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
camasaiścamasādhvaryurjuhotyadhvaryureva vā ।
saṃjñāviśeṣādādyo astu maivamadhvaryusaṃjñayā ।
viśeṣasyānapekṣatvāttenānyasyā apekṣaṇāt ।
adhvaryurjuhuyācchaktestadaśaktau paro api vā ।

acamasādhvaryuḥ' ityevaṃvidhasaṃjñāviśeṣāccamasādhvaryava eva camasairjuhuyuḥ - iti cet ।
maivam ।
adhvaryusaṃjñāyā nirapekṣatvena prabalatvāt ।
kevalādhvaryau camasādhvaryuṣu cānugato adhvaryuśabdaḥ sāmānyarūpaḥ ।
camasaśabdastu camasādhvaryuṣveveti viśeṣarūpaḥ ।
taṃ ca viśeṣamanapekṣyaivādhvaryuśabda ṛtviksaṃjñārūpeṇa vartituṃ prabhavati ।
camasaśabdastu sāmānyavācinamadhvaryuśabdamapekṣyaiva puruṣeṣu saṃjñā bhavati ।
tathā sati aādhvaryavo homaḥ' ityanayāṃ nirapekṣayāṃ prabalayā samākhyayādhvaryureva satyāṃ śaktau camasairjuhuyāt ।
grahahomavyāpṛtatvena kadācidaśaktau camasādhvaryavo juhuyuḥ ।
vedopadeśāt pūrvavadvedānyatve yathopadeśaṃ syuḥ ।
tadguṇād vā svadharmaḥ syād adhikārasāmarthyāt sahāṅgair avyaktaḥ śeṣe ।

-
trayoviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
śyena udgātṛvedokto vājapeyo yajuṣyam ।
udgātrādhvaryuṇā kāryau yathāprakṛti vāgrimaḥ ।
ākhyāviśeṣādākhyāyāḥ pūrvabhāvī hi codakaḥ ।
prakṛtāviva kartārastattaddharme vyavasthitāḥ ।

śyenayāgaḥ sāmavede samāmnāta iti tatratyāḥ sarve padārthā udgātrānuṣṭheyāḥ, bahiṣpavamānājyapṛṣṭhādistotreṣvivodgātratva samākhyāyāḥ śyone api samatvāt ।
tathā- yajurvede samāmnāto vājapeyaḥ sarvo apyadhvaryuṇaivānuṣṭheyaḥ ।
samākhyāvaśāt- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- śyenavājapeyau hi jyotiṣṭomavikārau ।
tatra codakastattatpadārthestaistaiḥ puruṣairanuṣṭheyatayā samarpayati ।
aṅgeṣvatidiṣṭeṣu paṣcātsāṅgapradhānānuṣṭhāpakasya prayogavacanasāya pravṛttiḥ ।
prayogavacanādhīnā tu samākhyātyantajaghanyā ।
tataḥ prabalacodakavaśātprakṛtāviva nānāvidhāḥ kartāraḥ svasvadharmeṣu vyavatiṣṭhante ।
iti śrīmādhavīya jaiminīyanyāyamālavistare tṛtīyādhyāyasya saptamaḥ pādaḥ

atha tṛtīyādhyāyasyāṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ ।
svāmikarma parikrayaḥ karmaṇas tadarthatvāt ।

-
aṣṭamapāde prathamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
dakṣiṇādiparikrītiṛtvijaḥ svāmino athavā ।
parikrayaḥ samākhyānādṛtvijaḥ syādyathetarat ।
parikrayātpurādhvaryuhotrādīnāmabhāvataḥ ।
parikrayaṇakartṛtvaṃ yajamānasya nartvijaḥ ।

dakṣiṇādānena karmakarāḥ parikretavyāḥ ।
tatra havistyāgavyatiriktaṃ sarvamārtvivyam- iti nirṇītam ।
dakṣiṇā ca dvādaśaśatarūpādhvaryuveda udgātṛvede ca samāmnātai ।
anvāhāryadakṣiṇādhvaryuvede ।
tataḥ samākhyayā parikratṛtvamṛtvijaḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
ṛtvijāṃ parikrayaṇottarakālīnānāṃ tatkartṛtvāsaṃbhavena yajamānasyaiva tatkartṛtvāt ।
vacanād itareṣāṃ syāt ।

dvitīyādhikaraṇamāracayati-
iṣṭakāvaradānaṃ kiṃ svāminaḥ syādutartvijaḥ ।
svāminaḥ pūrvavanmaivamadhvaryorvacanādayam ।

aya etāmiṣṭakāmupadadhyāt, sa trīnvārāndadyāt' ityupadhāturadhvaryorgotrayadānaṃ vācanikam ।
nahvasti vacanasyātibhāraḥ ।
saṃskārās tu puruṣasāmarthye yathāvedaṃ karmavadvyavatiṣṭheran ।
yājamānās tu tatpradhānatvāt karmavat ।
vyapadeśāc ca ।
guṇatvena tasya nirdeśaḥ ।
codanāṃ prati bhāvāc ca ।
atulyatvād asamānavidhānāḥ syuḥ ।

-
tṛtīyādhikaraṇamāracayati-
saṃskārā vapanādyāḥ kimadhvaryoḥ svāmino athavā ।
adhvaryostatra śaktatvāttadvedokteśca tasya te ।
saṃskārairyogyatāṃ prāpya svakārya kartumṛtvijaḥ ।
krīṇātyataḥ kriyā teṣāṃ saṃskriyā yajamānagā ।

aāpa undantu jīvase' ityādyāḥ saṃskāramantrāḥ ।
tadvidhayaścādhvaryuvede samāmnātāḥ- akeśaśmaśru vapate','nakhāni nikṛntate' iti ।
śaktaścādhvaryurvapanādau ।
tasmāt- tasyādhvaryoste vapanādisaṃskārāḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
vapanādisaṃskārā yajamānagatamālinyamapanīya yāgayogyatāmutpādayituṃ kriyante ।
tathā ca brāhmaṇam- akeśaśmaśru vapate ।
mṛtā vā eṣā tvagamedhyā yatkeśaśmaśru ।
mutāmeva tvacamamedhyāmapahatya yajñiyo bhūtvā medhamupaiti' iti ।
nahyadhvayuvapanena yajamānagatā mṛtā tvagapaiti ।
yogyasya hi karmādhikāra sati paścātprayāsarūpeṣu vyāpāreṣu svayamaśaktaḥ sankarmakarānṛtvijaḥ parikrīṇāti ।
loke api rogiṇaḥ svāmina auṣadhādyānayana eva bhṛtyo jīvitadānena parikrīyate ।
na tu tadauṣadhaṃ bhṛtyaḥ sevate ।
tasmāt- itarakriyartvijām, saṃskārastu yajamānasya ।
kvacittu ।
vacanādṛtvijāmapi saṃskāro astu ।
tapaś ca phalasiddhitvāl lokavat ।
vākyaśeṣaś ca tadvat ।
vacanād itareṣāṃ syāt ।

-
caturthādhikaraṇamāracayati-
nāśnāti dvayahamityetattapaḥ kasya tayordvayoḥ ।
duḥkhatvādbhoktṛsaṃskārādadhvaryoryujyate tapaḥ ।
phalāntarāyapāpasya nāśakatvena saṃskṛtiḥ ।
liṅgāttapaḥ svāmigāmi saṃskārāntaravattataḥ ।

jyotiṣṭhome- advyahaṃ nāśnāti' atryahaṃ nāśnāti'ityādinoktaṃ tapo aghvaryoryuktam ।
tasya duḥkhātmakatvena parikrītapuruṣaiḥ kartumucitatvāt ।
duḥkhatvādeva phalabhoktṛsaṃskāratvābhāvādyajamānasya na yuktam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
bhāvinaḥ sukharūpasya phalasya pratibandhakaṃ duḥkhajanakaṃ yatpāpaṃ tasya nāśakatvena duḥkharūpasyāpi tapasaḥ svāmisaṃskāratvasaṃbhavāt ।
asminnarthe vākyaśeṣagataṃ liṅgaṃ kalpasūtrakāreṇaivamudāhṛtam- ayadā vai dīkṣitaḥ kṛśo bhavati, atha medhyo bhavati ।
yadāsminnantarna kiṃcana bhavati, atha medhyo bhavati ।
yadāsya kṛṣṇaṃ cakṣuṣornaśyati, atha medhyo bhavati ।
yadāsya tvacāsthi saṃdhīyate, atha medhyo bhavati ।
pītvā dīkṣate, kṛśo yajate ।
yadasyāṅgānāṃ mīyate juhotyeva taditi vijñāyate' iti ।
na hi duḥkharūpaṃ tapo vinā duḥkhapradaṃ pāpaṃ naśyati ।
yathā pāṭanamantareṇa viṣavraṇānāṃ nopaśāntiḥ, tadvat ।
tasmāt- vapanādisaṃskāravattapo api yajamānasyaiva ।
guṇatvāc ca vedena na vyavasthā syāt ।

-
pañcamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
hiraṇyamālitādyāstu saṃskārā vacanānmatāḥ ।
ṛtvijāṃ te yathākhyānaṃ kartavyā nikhilairuta ।
ādya ākhyāvaśānmaivaṃ sarvasaṃnidhipāṭhataḥ ।
pratimukhyaṃ guṇāvṛtteḥ kartavyā nikhilairapi ।

vājapeye śrūyate- ahiraṇyamālina ṛtvijaḥ pracaranti' iti ।
śyene śrūyate- alohitoṣṇīṣā lohitavasanā nivītā ṛtvijaḥ pracaranti' iti ।
yadyapi hiraṇyamālitvādīnāṃ saṃskāratvādyajamānaviṣayatvaṃ pūrvanyāyena prāptam, tathāpi vacanādaya mṛtviksaṃskāraḥ ।
tatra hiraṇyamālitvaṃ yajurvedoktatvādadhvaryūṇāmeva, lohitoṣṇīṣādikaṃ sāmavedoktatvādudgātṝṇāmeva iti samākhyāvaśādabhyupeyam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
ahiraṇyamālina ṛtvijaḥ pracaranti' iti sarveṣāmṛtvijāṃ saṃnidhau paṭhyamāno hiraṇyamālitvasaṃskāraḥ saṃnidhinā samākhyāṃ bādhitvā sarvairapyṛtvigbhiḥ saṃbadhyate ।
kiṃca- saṃrakāryatvādṛtvijāṃ prādhānye sati pratipradhānaṃ guṇāvṛttyā sarveṣāmapyṛtvijāṃ hiraṇyamālitvādisaṃskāro abhyupatevyaḥ ।
tathā kāmo arthasaṃyogāt ।
vyapadeśād itareṣāṃ syāt ।

-
ṣaṣṭhādhikaraṇamāracayati-
vṛṣṭikāmī sado nīcairminuyāditi kāmanā ।
adhvaryoḥ svāmino vā'dyo vākyānmātustaducyate ।
parasmaipadato adhvaryuvyāpārasya parārthatā ।
pratītāto vākyabādhe tapovatsvāmino astu tat ।

jyotiṣṭhome śrūyate- ayadi kāmayeta- varṣukaḥ parjanyaḥ syāt- iti nīcaiḥ sado minuyāt' iti ।
-yathā purastātpaścāccāvasthitau havirdhānaprācīnavaṃśāvuccaiḥ, tathā sado noccaṃ, kiṃtu nīcaiḥ kāryam- ityarthaḥ ।
atra- vṛṣṭikāmanādhvaryoryuktā ।
ayaḥ kāmayet, sa minuyāt' iti vākyena kāmayitṛmātrorekatvāvagamāt ।
mātṛtvaṃ cādhvaryorityabivādam ।
tasmāt- sa kāmayitā- iti cet ।
maivam ।
aminuyāt' iti parasmaipadenādhvaryuvyāpāraphalasya paragāmitā pratīyate ।
tato vṛṣṭilakṣaṇaphalasya yajamānagāmitvātparasmaipadaśrutyā vākyaṃ bādhitvā kāmasya yajamānakartṛkatvaṃ draṣṭavyam ।
- ayajamānakāmitāṃ vṛṣṭiṃ parjanyaḥ saṃpādayatu' ityeva yo adhvaryuḥ kāmayate, sa nīcairminuyāt, iti vākyaṃ vyākhyeyam ।
- aevaṃvidudvātā'tmane vā yajamānāya vā yaṃ kāmaṃ kāmayate, tamāgāyati' iti ṛtvijo api kāmaḥ- iti cet ।
tarhi tasminnudgīthopāsane vacanādṛtvijo api phalamastu ।
mantrāś cākarmakaraṇās tadvat ।
viprayoge ca darśanāt ।

saptamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
āyurdā iti mantroktiḥ kasyādhvaryoḥ samākhyayā ।
tadbādhe liṅgataḥ svāmigāmitā kāmabanmatā ।

idamāmnāyate-'āyurdā agne asyāyurme dehi' iti ।
tasyaitasya mantrasya pāṭho adhvaryoryajamānasya vā -ityayaṃ saṃśayaḥ akasya' ityanena padena sūcitaḥ ।
asminmantre aāyurme dehi' iti phalasya svātmasaṃbandhaḥ pratīyate ।
sa ca yajamānasya yuktaḥ, nādhvaryoḥ ।
tasmāt- kāmavanmantro api yājamānaḥ ।
dvyāmnāteṣūbhau dvyāmnānasyārthavattvāt ।

aṣṭhamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
vājasya metyamuṃ brūyādeko dvau vā kṛtārthataḥ ।
ekaḥ kāṇḍadvaye pāṭhādadhvaryusvāmināvubhau ।

darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ- avājasya mā prasavena' ityayaṃ mantro adhvaryukāṇḍe yajamānakāṇḍe cā'mnātaḥ ।
tatraikena paṭhite sati mantrasya caritārthatvāditarastaṃ na paṭhet- iti cet ।
maivam ।
kāṇḍāntarapāṭhavaiyarythaprasaṅgāt ।
tasmādubhābhyāṃ paṭhanīyaḥ ।
tayoḥ paṭhatorāśayabhedo asti ।
aanena mantreṇa prakāśitamarthamanuṣṭhāsyāmi' ityadhvaryurmanute ।
aatra na pramadiṣyāmi' iti yajamānaḥ ।
jñāte ca vācanaṃ na hy avidvān vihito asti ।

navamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
vācayetsvāminaṃ jñājñau vācamīyau jña eva vā ।
aviśeṣādubhau jñasya svāmitvādvācayedamum ।

vājapeye śrūyate-'kḷptīryajamānaṃ vācayati' iti ।
aāryuyajñena kalpatām' ityādayo mantrāḥ kḷptayaḥ ।
tatra- mantratadarthābhijñamanabhijñaṃ cobhāvapi vācayet ।
avidvāsaṃ vācayet' ityevaṃ viśeṣasyāśravaṇāt ।
anabhijñaṃ tadaiva śikṣayitvāpi vācayituṃ śakyatvāt- iti cet ।
maivam ।
adhyayanavidhibalādadhītavedasya viditavedārthasyaiva yajamānatvāt ।
tasmāt- abhijñameva vācayetu ।
yājamāne samākhyānāt karmāṇi yājamānaṃ syuḥ ।
adhvaryur vā tadartho hi nyāyapūrve samākhyānam ।

-
daśamādhikaraṇamāracayati-
vatsaṃ copasṛjettadvadukhāṃ cādhiśrayoditi ।
dvādaśadvaṃdvakarmaitatsvāmino vetarasya vā ।
ādyaḥ pāṭhātsvāmikāṇḍe tādarthyena parikrayāt ।
mahākāṇḍoktito antyo astu dvaṃdvataivātra kīrtyate ।

darśapūrṇamāsayoryājamāne kāṇḍe śrūyate- advādaśa dvaṃdvāni darśapūrṇamāsayostāni saṃpādyāni- ityāhuḥ- vatsaṃ copāvasṛjati, ukhāṃ cādhiśrayati' ayaṃ ca hanti, dṛṣadau ca samāhanti' ityādi ।
tatra- palāśaśākhayā vatsāpākaraṇamekaṃ karma, dohanena saṃpāditaṃ kṣīraṃ dhārayituṃ piṭharasthāpanamaparaṃ karma, tadetadubhavamekaṃ dvaṃdvam ।
tathā vrīhīṇāmavaghātaḥ, dṛṣadupalayoḥ pāṣāṇāntareṇa samāghātaḥ, ityetadubhayaṃ dvitīyaṃ dvaṃdvam ।
evaṃ dvādaśa karmadvaṃdvānyanuṣṭheyānyāmnātāni ।
teṣāṃ yājamāne kāṇḍe paṭhitatvātsamākhyayā yajamānena tānyanuṣṭheyāni- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- yajamānasya yāni kāryāṇi, tānyanuṣṭhātumeva parikrītā ṛtvijaḥ ।
kiṃca- yajurvede yājamānamidamavāntara kāṇḍam, mahākāṇḍaṃ tvādhvaryavameva ।
tatraivaite vatsāpākaraṇādayo dharmā āmnātāḥ ।
tasmādardhvayureva tānanutiṣṭhet ।
yājamāne tu kāṇḍe na yevāmanuṣṭhānaprakāraścoditaḥ, kiṃtu parigaṇanayā dvaṃdvatāsaṃpādanamātramāmnātam ।
tena yajamānastāmānupūrvī manasi nidhāyādhvaryoranuṣṭhāne pramādarāhityamanusaṃdhātuṃ prabhavati ।
tasmādadhvaryorevānuṣṭhānam ।
vipratiṣedhe karaṇaḥ samavāyaviśeṣād itaram anyas teṣāṃ yato viśeṣaḥ syāt ।

-
ekādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
yo hotādhvaryureva syādityādhvaryavamācaran ।
hautraṃ kuryānna vā tyāgahetvamāvātkaroti tat ।
hotaiko yugapatkarmadvayaṃ kartu nahi prabhuḥ ।
tyajoccodakataḥ prāptaṃ hautraṃ vācanikāryakṛt ।

agnīṣomīyavaśau aparivīrasi' ityanena karaṇamantreṇādhvaryuryūpasya raśanayā pariṣyāṇaṃ karoti ।
tadānīṃ kriyamāṇaṃ tatparivyaṇaṃ hotā ayuvā suvāsāḥ'- ityanena mantreṇānuvadati ।
tadetadubhayaṃ codakaparamparayā kuṇḍapāyināmayane prāptam ।
tatrādhvaryorhotuśca samāsa āmnātaḥ- ayo hotā so adhvaryuḥ' iti ।
hotāramanūṣṭhā dhvaryutvavidhānādadhvaryukārye hotrānuṣṭheyam ।
tataḥ aparivīrasi' ityanena karaṇamantreṇa hotā yūpaparivyāṇaṃ kurvīta ।
tadānīṃ svasya codakataḥ prāptaṃ hautramapi hotā na tyajet ।
nahi tyāgahetuṃ kaṃcinniṣedhaṃ paśyāmaḥ ।
tasmātkriyamāṇaṃ tatparivyāṇaṃ ayuvā struṣāsāḥ' ityanena mantreṇa hotānuvadet- iti prāpte-
brūmaḥ- dvayoradhvaryuhotrorucitaṃ karmadvayameko hotā yugapatkartu na śaknoti ।
tato anyatarasyāvaśyaṃbhāvini tyāge codakataḥ prāptaṃ hautrameva tyajet ।
ādvayava tu ayo hotā so adhvaryuḥ' ityanena prāpitatvādanuṣṭheyam ।
praiṣeṣu ca parādhikārāt ।

dvādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
prokṣaṇyāsādanaṃ kuryādadhvaryuritaro athavā ।
ākhyayā'dyaḥ sādayeti preṣito anyo astu liṅgataḥ ।

darśapūrṇamāsayoḥ- prokṣaṇīnāṃ kenacitpātreṇa vedyāmātādanaṃ śrutam ।
tadetadyajurvedoktatvādādhvaryam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
praiṣamantravirodhaprasaṅgāt ।
aprokṣaṇīrāsādaya ।
idmāvarhirupatādava ।
agnīdagnīnvihara ।
varhiḥ stṛṇīhi' ityādiṣvādhvaryaveṣu praiṣamantreṣu śrūyamāṇamāgnīṃprasaṃbodhanaṃ madhyamapuruṣaścānyena tadanuṣṭhāne satyupapadyate ।
tasmāt- nā'dhvarthavam ।
adhvaryus tu darśanāt ।
gauṇo vā karmasāmānyāt ।

trayodaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
agnītpreṣyadutādhvaryuragnīdastvavirodhataḥ ।
ākhyāvirodhādadhvaryuḥ praiṣadvārār'thakṛdyataḥ ।

yathā prokṣaṇīrāgnīdhra āsādayati, tathā praiṣamantramapyāgnīdhra eva paṭhatu ।
virodhābhāvāt - iti cet ।
maivam ।
ādhvaryavasamākhyāyāḥ pūrvodāhṛtasaṃbodhanamadhyamapuruṣayośca virodhāt ।
na ca - prokṣaṇyāsādanādīnāma dhvaryukartṛkatvābhāve api samākhyāvirodhastadavasthaḥ- iti vācyam ।
praiṣadvārā prayojakakartṛtve api tadavirodhāt ।
tasmāt - adhvaryoreva praiṣamantraḥ ।
dghasūtrāṇi -)
ṛtvik phalaṃ karaṇeṣv arthatvāt ।
svāmino vā tadarthatvāt ।
liṅgadarśanāc ca ।

caturdaśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
mamāgna iti kasyātra phalaṃ liṅgena vaktṛgam ।
śrutyā svāmini na krīte liṅgaṃ tatropacaryatām ।

amamāgne varco vihaveṣvastu' ityayamāhavanīyasyānvādhāne karaṇabhūto mantro adhva- ।
rpuṇā paṭhyate ।
aviśiṣṭaṃ havanaṃ yeṣāṃ yajñānāṃ te vihavāsteṣu varcastejasopalakṣitaṃ yatphalaṃ tanmamāstu' ityanena liṅgena mantramuccārayituradhvaryostatphalam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
adarśapūrṇamāsābhyāṃ svargakāmo yajeta' ityātmanepadaśrutyā sāṅgapradhānaphalasya yajamānagāmitvaṃ pratīyate ।
na ca parikrītasyādhvaryordakṣiṇātiktaphalasaṃbandho nyāyyaḥ ।
tasmāt- śrutinyāyābhyāṃ viruddhaṃ talliṅgaṃ yajamānaparatvenopacaraṇīyam ।
amadīyayajamānasya tadvarco astu' iti hyupacāraḥ ।
