tasmāt- yajamānena pāṭhyeṣu aāyurdā agne asyāyurme dehi' ityādiṣu kriyamāṇānuvādiṣu pratyagāśīrmantreṣu śrutaṃ phalaṃ yathā yājamānam, tathaivādhvaryuṇā pāṭhyeṣu karaṇamantreṣu śrutamapi phalaṃ yājamānameva ।
karmārthaṃ tu phalaṃ teṣāṃ svāminaṃ pratyarthavattvāt ।

pañcadaśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
mā mā saṃtāptamityetatkasminsvāmini pūrvavat ।
adhvaryāvastu tattena svāmikarmopayogataḥ ।

darśapūrṇamāsayorāghārahomārthamājyapūrṇau strukstruvau gṛhītvā nābhisamīpe hastena dhārayate ।
tatrāyaṃ karaṇamantro adhvaryuṇā paṭhyate - aagnāviṣṇū mā vāmavakramivaṃ vijihāthāṃ mā mā saṃtāptaṃ lokaṃ me lokakṛtau kuṇutam' iti ।
abho strukstruvarūpāvagnāviṣṇū yuvāṃ nābhideśe dhārayannahamadhvaryurmā vāmavakramiṣaṃ yuvayoratikramaṃ na kṛtavānasmi ।
yuvāṃ ca matto viyuktau mā bhavatam ।
tato māṃ dehadhāriṇaṃ mā saṃtāptaṃ mama dehe saṃtāpaṃ jvarādirūpaṃ mā kurutam ।
sthānakṛtau yuvāmāghārahomāya sthānaṃ kurutam' ityarthaḥ ।
tatra pūrvoktavarconyāyena saṃtāpābhāvo api yajamānasyaiva, na tvadhvaryoḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
adhvaryāvasaṃtapte satyavighnena svāminaḥ karma samāpyate ।
tasmāt - adhvayurgato api saṃtāpābhāvo yajamānasyaiva phalam - iti nātra macchabdasyopacāraḥ ।
vyapadeśāc ca ।

ṣoḍaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
bhadraṃ tannau sahetyetatkasminsvāmini yujyate ।
dvitvaśrutyā dvayoretadadhvaryuyajamānayoḥ ।

jyotiṣṭome havirdhānamaṇḍape somābhiṣavādhārayoḥ phalakayoradhastāccatasṛṣvāgneyyādividikṣu catvāra uparavanāmakā gartā aratnimātrakhātā adhobhāge parasparaṃ militā ūrdhvabhāge parasparaṃ prādeśamātravyavahitā vartante ।
teṣvekasminnuparave yajamāno dakṣiṇahastaṃ prasārayati, tathaivādhvaryuranyasminsvahastaṃ prasāryādhastādyajamānahastaṃ gṛhṇāti ।
tadā yajamānaḥ akimatra' ityanena mantreṇa phalaṃ pṛcchati ।
adhvaryuśca abhadram-' ityanena mantreṇottaraṃ brūte ।
tato yajamānaḥ atannau saha - a ityanena mantreṇa tatphalaṃ svakīyatvena svī karoti ।
tasmāt- yajamānasyaiva tat -
iti cet ।
maivam ।
anau' ityanena dvivacanena, asaha' ityanena cobhayagāmitayaiva svīkārāt ।
dravyasaṃskāraḥ prakāraṇāviśeṣāt sarvakarmaṇām ।
nirdeśāt tu vikṛtāv apūrvasyānadhikāraḥ ।

-
saptadaśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
dharmāṇāṃ prakṛtisthānāṃ vikṛtāvatideśataḥ ।
prāptirviśeṣato vā'dyo viśeṣasyānirūpaṇāt ।
prakṛtau kāryakṛddharmā vikṛtau syurna cetare ।
yūpāvaṭāstṛtiḥ kārya na hi prākṛtabarhiṣaḥ ।

darśapūrṇamāsayorvedidharmā barhirrdhamāśca havirāsādanādayo aṅgapradhānārthā iti pūrvatra nirṇītam ।
te ca dharmā vikṛtāvatiddiśyamānā niyāmakābhāvātsarve apyatidiśyantām- iti prāpte, -
brūmaḥ- kāryamatra niyāmakam ।
prakṛtau hi havirāsādanaṃ vedikāryam ।
tacca vikṛtāvapi prāpyamāṇaṃ svasiddhayekhananādīnvedidharmānprāpayati ।
yūpāvaṭāstaraṇarūpaṃ tu kārya na prakṛtāvasti ।
darśapūrṇamāsayoryūpāvaṭābhāvāt ।
tarcca''staraṇakārye vikṛtau vidhīyamānamapyaprākṛtakāryatayā prākṛtāllaṃvanādīnvarhiḥ saṃskārānna prāpayanti ।
tasmātprakṛtigatāḥ kāryakṛddharmā eva vikṛtau prāpyante ।
virodhe ca śrutiviśeṣād avyaktaḥ śeṣe ।

aṣṭādaśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
yadvarhistatpavitrārtha na vā'dyastasya saṃbhavāt ।
saṃskṛtaṃ staraṇe kṣīṇaṃ pavitraṃ tvanyato bhavet ।

darśapūrṇamāsayorāmananti- asamāvapracchinnāgnau darmau prādeśamātrau pavitre karoti' iti ।
tatra- yadetadvedistaraṇārtha lavanasaṃskṛtaṃ barhiḥ, tena pavitrasaṃbhavādāstaraṇavatpavitramapi barhipaḥ kāryam - iti cet ।
maivam ।
āstaraṇa eva saṃskṛtasya sarvasya barhiṣa upakṣīṇatvāt ।
na hi avediṃ stṛṇāti' iti vihitasya staraṇasyākasmādbarhirekadeśe saṃkoco yuktaḥ ।
tasmāt- yathā yūpāvaṭamasaṃskṛtena barhiṣā stṛṇāti, tathā pavitraniṣpattirapi śāstrīyalavanādisaṃskārarahitaiḥ paribhojanīyanāmakairdarbheḥ saṃpādanīyā ।
apanayas tv ekadeśasya vidyamānasaṃyogāt ।

-
ekonaviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
puroḍāśasya śakalamaindravāyavapātrake ।
avadadhyātpuroḍāśo navo atha savanīyakaḥ ।
siddhasya yajanārtatvānnavaṃ saṃpādya tatkriyā ।
savanīyena tatkārye saṃskāryatvāddvitīyayā ।

jyotiṣṭome śrūyate - apuroḍāśaśakalamaindravāyavasya pātre nidadhāti' iti ।
tatra- stravanīyapuroḍāśasya śakalaṃ yadyapi niṣpannam, tathāpi tasya yajamārthatvena saṃskṛtabarhirbadupakṣayānnūtanaṃ kaṃcitpuroḍāśaṃ saṃpādya tadīyaśaphalasyaindravāyavapātraprakṣepakriyā kartavyā - iti cet ।
maivam ।
savanīyapuroḍāśaśakalenaitannidhānaṃ kartavyam ।
kutaḥ ।
saṃskāryatvāt ।
aśakalaṃ nidadhāti' iti dvitīyayā saṃskāryatvaṃ gamyate ।
iṣṭaśiṣṭasya hi pratipattirūpaḥ saṃskāraḥ ।
na cātra kṛtsnaṃ yajanārtham ।
avadānasyeyattapāpuroḍāśabhāgasyāvaśeṣitatvāt ।
yathātra pūrvasiddhapuroḍāśaśakalam, tathā'dhānā āścinapātre' apayasyāṃ maitrāvaruṇapātre' ityatrāpi pūrvaśeṣasyaiva prakṣepaḥ ।
vikṛtau sarvārthaḥ śeṣaḥ prakṛtitvāt ।
mukhyārtho vāṅgasyācoditatvāt ।

-
viṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
kāmyā upāṃśu yaṣṭhavyāḥ kiṃ tadaṅgapradhānayoḥ ।
pradhāna eva vā nātra viśeṣoktirato dvayoḥ ।
mukhyānāmeva kāmyatvātteṣveva paricodanā ।
aṅgānāmatathābhāvādupāṃśutvaṃ pradhānagam ।

idamāmnāyate - ayajñātharvaṇaṃ vai kāmyā iṣṭayaḥ, tā upāṃśu ṣaṣṭavyāḥ' iti ।
atharvavedoktakarmavadyajñeṣu kāmyā iṣṭayo gomyāḥ ।
tasmāttāsāmupāṃśutvaṃ yuktamityarthaḥ ।
yathā vedidharmāṇāṃ barhirrdhamāṇāṃ cāṅgapradhānayoḥ samāno vidhiḥ, tathopāṃśutvasyāpi ।
nahyatra kaścidviśeṣa āmnātaḥ- iti cet ।
maivam ।
kāmyatvasyaivātra viśeṣaniyāmekatvāt ।
na tvaṅgānāṃ kāmyatvamasti ।
karaṇapauṣkalyasaṃpādakānāṃ teṣāṃ phale sākṣātsaṃbandhābhāvāt ।
tataḥ- sākṣātphalasādhane pradhāna evopāṃśutvam ।
aṅgeṣu tu tattadvedānusāreṇa dhvaniviśeṣaḥ ।
saṃnidhānāviśeṣād asaṃbhave tadaṅgānām ।
ādhāne api tatheti cet ।
nāprakaraṇatvād aṅgasyātannimittatvāt ।

-
ekaviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
navanītaṃ śyena ājyaṃ mukhye aṅge vāstu mukhyagam ।
vidheyamājyamapraptaṃ dṛtisthanavanītakam ।
mukhyaḥ somavikāro aṅge codakaprāptamājyakam ।
anūdya dṛtisaṃsthānaṃ navanītaguṇo vidhiḥ ।

śyene śrūyate - adṛtinavanītamājyaṃ bhavati' iti ।
dṛtau ciraṃ saṃgṛhītaṃ navanītaṃ yasyā'jyasya prakṛtidravyaṃ tadetadīdṛśamājyaṃ mānāntareṇa pūrvamaprāptatvātpradhānakarmaṇi vidheyam- iti cet ।
maivam ।
pradhānaśyenasya somayāgavikāratvenā'jyāpekṣāyā abhāvāt ।
aṅgeṣviṣṭiviśeṣeṣu codakaprāptasyā'jyasya prakṛtidravyatvena yathoktanavanītaguṇo vidhīyate ।
tatkāle vā liṅgadarśanāt ।
sarveṣāṃ vāviśeṣāt ।
nyāyokte liṅgadarśanam ।

dvāviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati-
sutyākālagatāṅgeṣu guṇaḥ sarveṣu voditaḥ ।
ādyo vaiśeṣikāṅgatvādvākyātsarvāṅgasaṃgatiḥ ।

yo ayaṃ śyenasyāṅgeṣu dṛtinavanītatvaguṇo vihitaḥ so ayaṃ sutyākālīneṣveva savanīyapaśutatpuroḍāśarūpeṣvaṅgeṣu, na tu kālāntaravartidīkṣaṇīyādyaṅgeṣu ।
vimato guṇaḥ sutyākālīnāṅgamātragaḥ, śyenavaiśeṣikatvāt, paśusāhityavat ।
yathā asaha paśūnālabhate' iti vihitaṃ paśusāhityaṃ śyena eva viśeṣatvenocyamānaṃ sutyākālīneṣveva savanīyapaśuṣvavasthitam, tathā - navanītamapi- iti prāpte -
brūmaḥ- ayadājyaṃ taddṛtinavanītam' itivākyena sarvāṅgatājyaviṣayatvapratītāvanumānaṃ kālātyayāpadiṣṭam ।
tasmāt- sarveṣvaṅgeṣu tannavanītam ।
māṃsaṃ tu savanīyānāṃ codanāviśeṣāt ।
bhaktir asaṃnidhāvanyāyyeti cet ।
syāt prakṛtiliṅgād vairājavat ।

-
trayoviṃśādhikaraṇamāracayati -
śākyāyane puroḍāśāstarasā iti māṃsatā ।
sarvatra savanīye vā sarvatra navanītavat ।
tarasāḥ savanīyāḥ syuriti tatsaṃnidhiḥ śrutaḥ ।
puroḍāśasya māṃsatvaṃ teṣvevāto niyamyate ।

ṣaṭtriṃśatsu saṃvatsareṣvanuṣṭheyaṃ śākyāyanam ।
tatra śrūyate - saṃsthito ahani gṛhapatirmṛgayāṃ yāti, sa yānmṛgānhanti, teṣāṃ tarasāḥ savamīyāḥ puroḍāśā bhavanti' iti ।
tatra- yathā navanītaṃ sarveṣvaṅgeṣu niviṣṭam, tathā māṃsatvamapi sarveṣu puroḍāśeṣu niviśate - iti cet ।
maivam ।
tadā hi aye puroḍāśāste tarasāḥ' iti vacanavyaktau vyavahitānvayaḥ syāt ।
tarasaśabdapuroḍāśaśabdayormadhye savanīyaśabdena vyavadhānāt ।
iha tu atarasāḥ savanīyāḥ' ityanayoḥ saṃnidhiḥ śrūyate ।
tathā sati aye savanīyāste tarasāḥ' ityanena saṃnidhyanugṛhītena vākyena māṃsatvaṃ savanīyapuroḍāśeṣveva niyamyate ।
iti śrīmādhavīye jaiminīyanyāyamālāvistare tṛtīyādhyāyasyāṣṭamaḥ pādaḥ
samāptaścāyaṃ tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ
